id="8d3b9f56-7166-4e2c-ab53-048fc813811b">短い文を組み合わせて、静かで落ち着いたお正月の雰囲気を表現しています。</p></li></ul></li></ol><hr><ol name="1f82de02-c9b4-46b8-be1d-7a2b8e997205" id="1f82de02-c9b4-46b8-be1d-7a2b8e997205"><li><p name="77af6800-ecd4-4c96-b731-993ad5d7dcc9" id="77af6800-ecd4-4c96-b731-993ad5d7dcc9">質問文 (英語)：Which festival or holiday do you like the most?</p></li><li><p name="5518f85b-a075-4a8d-b0b8-57156ae7ab5e" id="5518f85b-a075-4a8d-b0b8-57156ae7ab5e">模範解答 (英語)：I like the summer Obon festival the most. There are traditional dances called Bon Odori and beautiful lanterns. The atmosphere is festive and wearing a yukata is fun.</p></li><li><p name="236de828-3649-4d69-8804-665509538118" id="236de828-3649-4d69-8804-665509538118">語彙・表現：</p><ul name="90706688-8940-4cfe-8bae-2f7e06b6a710" id="90706688-8940-4cfe-8bae-2f7e06b6a710"><li><p name="53817659-9caf-46c8-9e57-5493f3981e27" id="53817659-9caf-46c8-9e57-5493f3981e27"><strong>Obon festival (お盆祭り)</strong>：先祖を供養する日本の夏の行事。</p></li><li><p name="09f10d78-c29d-4e37-9f79-056d3b28018e" id="09f10d78-c29d-4e37-9f79-056d3b28018e"><strong>Bon Odori (盆踊り)</strong>：お盆に踊られる伝統的な踊り。</p></li><li><p name="c93494d5-3564-4695-83d6-ca2fa5fb5614" id="c93494d5-3564-4695-83d6-ca2fa5fb5614"><strong>lanterns (提灯)</strong>：祭りで灯される明かり。</p></li><li><p name="bce2405f-276b-4d69-a37f-b2ceaae5ffdb" id="bce2405f-276b-4d69-a37f-b2ceaae5ffdb"><strong>yukata (浴衣)</strong>：夏祭りで着る伝統的な服。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="1b675389-2a01-44bd-b23c-d861bf23cbac" id="1b675389-2a01-44bd-b23c-d861bf23cbac">文構造と接続表現：</p><ul name="deab329f-60da-42c9-9392-c28c047b6ceb" id="deab329f-60da-42c9-9392-c28c047b6ceb"><li><p name="3180cc6c-bf6e-466c-8ae9-464b8b2fd285" id="3180cc6c-bf6e-466c-8ae9-464b8b2fd285"><strong>"and"</strong> で盆踊りと提灯を並列しています。</p></li><li><p name="5df34124-35bd-437f-a6da-1c8f26a53f88" id="5df34124-35bd-437f-a6da-1c8f26a53f88"><strong>"called"</strong> で盆踊りを補足説明しています。</p></li><li><p name="f136131e-c9ba-41de-a3ea-4087bb55666f" id="f136131e-c9ba-41de-a3ea-4087bb55666f"><strong>"and wearing a yukata is fun."</strong> で二つの感想（祭りの雰囲気、浴衣の楽しさ）を<strong>and</strong>でつないでいます。</p></li><li><p name="55bc40ed-7e61-47ab-819f-c44a0eeade58" id="55bc40ed-7e61-47ab-819f-c44a0eeade58"><strong>現在形</strong>で好みを表現しています。</p></li></ul></li></ol><hr><h3 name="bde918d2-ccce-448e-916e-90271c77d424" id="bde918d2-ccce-448e-916e-90271c77d424">日常生活 (Daily Routine)</h3><ol name="75c8d875-aa0a-440d-be04-de603badf49d" id="75c8d875-aa0a-440d-be04-de603badf49d"><li><p name="91642928-e82f-4ba2-bded-3063f44b863a" id="91642928-e82f-4ba2-bded-3063f44b863a">質問文 (英語)：What time do you usually get up?</p></li><li><p name="478df088-e04b-4897-928c-ab32ddda31b3" id="478df088-e04b-4897-928c-ab32ddda31b3">模範解答 (英語)：I usually wake up around 7:00 AM. I set an alarm clock to make sure I wake up on time. This gives me time to start my day calmly.</p></li><li><p name="0ef5117d-475b-4d83-9233-0192e26def04" id="0ef5117d-475b-4d83-9233-0192e26def04">語彙・表現：</p><ul name="e4290184-38fd-435c-b786-48c0969f8ab0" id="e4290184-38fd-435c-b786-48c0969f8ab0"><li><p name="b95e7b6c-8b27-4239-b5ad-3a2b6bc1b904" id="b95e7b6c-8b27-4239-b5ad-3a2b6bc1b904"><strong>wake up (起きる)</strong>：起床を表す動詞。</p></li><li><p name="6697a5cf-d179-4e32-9239-57aba29ced2c" id="6697a5cf-d179-4e32-9239-57aba29ced2c"><strong>alarm clock (目覚まし時計)</strong>：起床用の機械。</p></li><li><p name="425a84be-73b8-4a5e-82ab-d31c2c8859fc" id="425a84be-73b8-4a5e-82ab-d31c2c8859fc"><strong>on time (時間通りに)</strong>：定刻に行動することを表します。</p></li><li><p name="88bc448b-6d45-4947-973c-4e59c8d4ee8c" id="88bc448b-6d45-4947-973c-4e59c8d4ee8c"><strong>calmly (落ち着いて)</strong>：落ち着いた状態で始める様子を表します。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="0b0f702b-f10d-4d15-8cb1-e51b0cdc756d" id="0b0f702b-f10d-4d15-8cb1-e51b0cdc756d">文構造と接続表現：</p><ul name="baf0ac32-441b-49d1-abab-1a2b388dc120" id="baf0ac32-441b-49d1-abab-1a2b388dc120"><li><p name="32d6334a-79a0-49dc-8e72-cc8f47dbb772" id="32d6334a-79a0-49dc-8e72-cc8f47dbb772"><strong>"I usually wake up..."</strong> で普段の起床時間を述べています。</p></li><li><p name="e771001f-0f86-4653-a6af-3b00423350f7" id="e771001f-0f86-4653-a6af-3b00423350f7"><strong>"I set an alarm clock..."</strong> で習慣や対策を説明しています。</p></li><li><p name="123a073e-2ede-429a-87e8-84f0f870c34d" id="123a073e-2ede-429a-87e8-84f0f870c34d"><strong>現在形</strong>で日常的な行動を述べています。</p></li><li><p name="331a12b4-552d-4674-8a5d-b05f7e25c07d" id="331a12b4-552d-4674-8a5d-b05f7e25c07d"><strong>短い文</strong>で明瞭に答えています。</p></li></ul></li></ol><hr><ol name="b229aeed-6296-4df1-83fc-e56fd329edb4" id="b229aeed-6296-4df1-83fc-e56fd329edb4"><li><p name="c7643bb2-6724-41f0-bb50-8d7c69a6082a" id="c7643bb2-6724-41f0-bb50-8d7c69a6082a">質問文 (英語)：What do you do in the morning after getting up?</p></li><li><p name="fcbe93bb-d847-46be-980d-7bc17301277f" id="fcbe93bb-d847-46be-980d-7bc17301277f">模範解答 (英語)：After getting up, I usually take a shower and have breakfast. Then I check my emails and get dressed for work. Drinking a cup of coffee helps me feel awake.</p></li><li><p name="c74265bb-8442-4054-b8e4-f7ed51a272d0" id="c74265bb-8442-4054-b8e4-f7ed51a272d0">語彙・表現：</p><ul name="758e823e-6639-4376-a6e4-91c8150d31b3" id="758e823e-6639-4376-a6e4-91c8150d31b3"><li><p name="7a7fe46a-7ec1-423a-a7b6-bfd4ca2eebe9" id="7a7fe46a-7ec1-423a-a7b6-bfd4ca2eebe9"><strong>take a shower (シャワーを浴びる)</strong>：朝の習慣を表すフレーズ。</p></li><li><p name="90796caa-cf91-40bb-b185-dd213cc395c9" id="90796caa-cf91-40bb-b185-dd213cc395c9"><strong>have breakfast (朝食を取る)</strong>：朝食を食べること。</p></li><li><p name="5fe2b67b-851b-4cae-a6d4-88107ac4e330" id="5fe2b67b-851b-4cae-a6d4-88107ac4e330"><strong>check my emails (メールを確認する)</strong>：メールをチェックして仕事を始めること。</p></li><li><p name="459d2232-39a1-4af2-8208-ab2f3d2d157e" id="459d2232-39a1-4af2-8208-ab2f3d2d157e"><strong>feel awake (目覚める)</strong>：目がしっかり覚めることを示します。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="f6b7a9f3-5d0c-4d17-b758-432aeb1faf00" id="f6b7a9f3-5d0c-4d17-b758-432aeb1faf00">文構造と接続表現：</p><ul name="b04fcfc4-27aa-467d-8a1c-a7224106ee36" id="b04fcfc4-27aa-467d-8a1c-a7224106ee36"><li><p name="187d8f5d-c7e8-4b0c-b1e8-30a101e1baa4" id="187d8f5d-c7e8-4b0c-b1e8-30a101e1baa4"><strong>"and"</strong> で複数の活動を並列しています。</p></li><li><p name="3513d70a-0c65-48ce-8c7f-c4bdfa91e77c" id="3513d70a-0c65-48ce-8c7f-c4bdfa91e77c"><strong>"Then"</strong> で次の行動へ順序を示しています。</p></li><li><p name="a4ffec24-ce34-4112-8cf0-169650983ffc" id="a4ffec24-ce34-4112-8cf0-169650983ffc"><strong>現在形</strong>で習慣を述べています。</p></li><li><p name="5d65be96-918e-4ac7-a501-f1f77aa750d4" id="5d65be96-918e-4ac7-a501-f1f77aa750d4"><strong>"helps me feel awake"</strong> で結果を説明しています。</p></li></ul></li></ol><hr><ol name="9fecc398-8632-4bab-95d8-9430e57e528b" id="9fecc398-8632-4bab-95d8-9430e57e528b"><li><p name="eae7dcd8-e654-4e24-8c89-8111fbf5614c" id="eae7dcd8-e654-4e24-8c89-8111fbf5614c">質問文 (英語)：Are you a morning person or a night person?</p></li><li><p name="7fd338e4-0034-49c2-be0e-1a58abb065f7" id="7fd338e4-0034-49c2-be0e-1a58abb065f7">模範解答 (英語)：I'm definitely a morning person. I feel more active and productive in the morning. In the evening, I prefer to relax by reading or watching TV.</p></li><li><p name="8840e8d5-0710-4acb-9f59-9a5e4f830c88" id="8840e8d5-0710-4acb-9f59-9a5e4f830c88">語彙・表現：</p><ul name="982e0548-6d77-4259-8520-364853bc4743" id="982e0548-6d77-4259-8520-364853bc4743"><li><p name="387fd455-0464-489b-a769-99f4fbdf4bfb" id="387fd455-0464-489b-a769-99f4fbdf4bfb"><strong>morning person (朝型の人)</strong>：朝に強く活発な人を指します。</p></li><li><p name="7090f01f-f79d-4475-b0b8-b77119ee896a" id="7090f01f-f79d-4475-b0b8-b77119ee896a"><strong>active (活動的な)</strong>：元気に動ける様子を表します。</p></li><li><p name="24f142c6-56d6-4226-8bc5-793dbdb683fb" id="24f142c6-56d6-4226-8bc5-793dbdb683fb"><strong>productive (生産的な)</strong>：効率よく活動できることを示します。</p></li><li><p name="49e4afcb-553d-44c1-ad49-4dfa0f92b148" id="49e4afcb-553d-44c1-ad49-4dfa0f92b148"><strong>relax (くつろぐ)</strong>：くつろいで過ごすことを示します。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="4ba09bb3-5aff-44e9-ad44-a0dd7571a79a" id="4ba09bb3-5aff-44e9-ad44-a0dd7571a79a">文構造と接続表現：</p><ul name="7f47d90b-11dd-44a3-9440-676f0ad107b9" id="7f47d90b-11dd-44a3-9440-676f0ad107b9"><li><p name="023bc8f3-d451-4f24-8ab9-583dd8fa54d1" id="023bc8f3-d451-4f24-8ab9-583dd8fa54d1"><strong>"I'm definitely a morning person."</strong> で確実な好みを述べています。</p></li><li><p name="b15460be-157b-4800-8e4f-21abee6b7a09" id="b15460be-157b-4800-8e4f-21abee6b7a09"><strong>"and"</strong> で二つの形容詞を並列しています。</p></li><li><p name="b144d994-f117-434d-a954-9274cf7d630c" id="b144d994-f117-434d-a954-9274cf7d630c"><strong>現在形</strong>で一般的な習慣を述べています。</p></li><li><p name="4f5b4584-a702-4ad8-9653-574df3e37ca6" id="4f5b4584-a702-4ad8-9653-574df3e37ca6"><strong>"In the evening, ..."</strong> で時間帯による対比を示しています。</p></li></ul></li></ol><hr><h2 name="85eee6c0-4405-4d88-bfc0-f316596d1efa" id="85eee6c0-4405-4d88-bfc0-f316596d1efa">Part2：ロングターン（長い回答）の構成とテンプレート</h2><figure name="f1fe8478-3e9f-491b-bb88-4fbd4ac572f8" id="f1fe8478-3e9f-491b-bb88-4fbd4ac572f8"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993359-fweiaEv10VWRkL6cjrZG4IxS.png" alt="" width="620" height="389"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="e7524f0f-2b64-409c-a4d6-68f320c2b678" id="e7524f0f-2b64-409c-a4d6-68f320c2b678">IELTSスピーキングのパート2では、面接官から渡されるトピックカードについて<strong>1分間準備</strong>し、<strong>2分間</strong>でスピーチを行います。 <br>回答は「導入→展開→結論」の型を意識し、<strong>5W1H</strong>（Who, What, Where, When, Why, How）で情報を整理して話すと効果的です。<br><br>冒頭では例えば“I’m going to tell you about…（～についてお話しします）”や“I’d like to talk about…（～についてお話ししたいと思います）”と切り出し、問題文をパラフレーズするとよいでしょう。<br><br>本論では過去の経験→現在（当時）→未来の展望の順に時系列で話題を展開し、最後に感想やまとめで締めくくります。<br><br>IELTS公式によれば、スピーキングの評価基準は「<strong>流暢さ・一貫性</strong>」「<strong>語彙力</strong>」「<strong>文法の範囲と正確さ</strong>」「<strong>発音</strong>」の4項目です。 <br>つまり、構成だけでなく適切な語彙や多様な文法表現を交えつつ、一貫性を持って話すことが求められます。</p><hr><p name="c06f147c-3476-4153-9283-cf7bcda63a3d" id="c06f147c-3476-4153-9283-cf7bcda63a3d"><strong>回答のコツ</strong>：</p><figure name="d7c4626e-5740-4b5a-9727-a41c021c373a" id="d7c4626e-5740-4b5a-9727-a41c021c373a"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993412-47DQTuZGL30jX6zeMqnFsfcb.png" alt="" width="620" height="344"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><ul name="a79fb7bf-15bd-4c62-9804-697a2092fc72" id="a79fb7bf-15bd-4c62-9804-697a2092fc72"><li><p name="723ae4d5-5cf0-4398-8cb1-b6424a550358" id="723ae4d5-5cf0-4398-8cb1-b6424a550358"><strong>構成を意識する</strong>：</p><ul name="94cf765c-649e-4bad-9866-9118a4308204" id="94cf765c-649e-4bad-9866-9118a4308204"><li><p name="0879fc28-ea63-480b-ae91-89d44aa04ee8" id="0879fc28-ea63-480b-ae91-89d44aa04ee8">回答は「導入→詳細→結論」の流れで組み立てます。</p><ul name="34ee2a02-8d7c-424c-974c-d64b8b242eae" id="34ee2a02-8d7c-424c-974c-d64b8b242eae"><li><p name="95cfd665-43e4-4104-8b73-0bc645eaf591" id="95cfd665-43e4-4104-8b73-0bc645eaf591">まずトピック全体を簡単に紹介し、次に要点ごとに具体的な内容（時系列や因果関係）を述べ、最後に感想や一般化した意見で締めくくります。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="19b75394-bae5-4113-b83b-e537994ff030" id="19b75394-bae5-4113-b83b-e537994ff030"><strong>テンプレート例</strong>：</p><ul name="96c9b241-91ed-4207-a865-245fd90a2267" id="96c9b241-91ed-4207-a865-245fd90a2267"><li><p name="b72326ee-a72b-41b1-9992-872a189b96e0" id="b72326ee-a72b-41b1-9992-872a189b96e0">導入：「One memorable trip I took was to Kyoto last autumn. I went there with my family for a week. I will talk about what we did, why it was special, and how it affected me.」</p></li><li><p name="70e26d1a-384e-49df-988d-c6d4233305a1" id="70e26d1a-384e-49df-988d-c6d4233305a1">内容展開：時系列で話を進めましょう。 <br>例：“Firstly, we arrived in Kyoto and visited famous temples. Then we tried local food. One highlight was...” のように、First/Firstly, Next, After that, Finally などの語で区切りを示す。</p></li><li><p name="8204df35-1609-404e-8d81-765f1e7924b5" id="8204df35-1609-404e-8d81-765f1e7924b5">結論：感想や学んだことを述べます。<br>例：“It was an amazing experience that showed me the beauty of Japanese culture.”</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="7a1acedb-6e8e-43c6-ac9c-fddf3088f4b2" id="7a1acedb-6e8e-43c6-ac9c-fddf3088f4b2"><strong>時間配分</strong>：</p><ul name="d2ee1c92-5232-4d54-91db-b32651c6d03b" id="d2ee1c92-5232-4d54-91db-b32651c6d03b"><li><p name="40a8ca10-d044-4643-b827-74365192d519" id="40a8ca10-d044-4643-b827-74365192d519">準備時間に要点を日本語で箇条書きし、各ポイントに使う英語表現を思い浮かべます。</p><ul name="77aa9d1b-6971-4ff1-85b7-c5c6b3728d97" id="77aa9d1b-6971-4ff1-85b7-c5c6b3728d97"><li><p name="453f2ad4-f609-47f2-922a-854275aef470" id="453f2ad4-f609-47f2-922a-854275aef470">2分を使い切るには、詳細（Who, What, When, Where, Why, How）を盛り込みつつ、冗長にならないよう注意。</p></li><li><p name="8fcf9db0-b120-435a-8d03-9de291f72d8d" id="8fcf9db0-b120-435a-8d03-9de291f72d8d">可能なら2分少しオーバーするくらいの長さで練習すると安心です。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="ac3a4910-4a5e-4f4a-bf5a-a28661b76b0c" id="ac3a4910-4a5e-4f4a-bf5a-a28661b76b0c"><strong>語彙・表現</strong>：</p><ul name="21082805-3322-475d-9670-874675587390" id="21082805-3322-475d-9670-874675587390"><li><p name="165aeb93-8e4d-47ec-9fc9-1f8acf61c9da" id="165aeb93-8e4d-47ec-9fc9-1f8acf61c9da">経験を表す動詞（traveled, visited, enjoyed など）</p></li><li><p name="7b1e446f-5fbd-4a8e-bdb9-b1cac88bce19" id="7b1e446f-5fbd-4a8e-bdb9-b1cac88bce19">感情を示す形容詞（memorable, excited など）</p></li><li><p name="7cfcdebe-59b8-4d84-a4b8-50295116ae09" id="7cfcdebe-59b8-4d84-a4b8-50295116ae09">場所・時期を表す語（last summer, traditional tea house など）を積極的に使います。</p><ul name="340405af-180d-4e10-97d5-107af2dac980" id="340405af-180d-4e10-97d5-107af2dac980"><li><p name="e4a88f31-cf23-4de9-9692-5856fe3c1c3e" id="e4a88f31-cf23-4de9-9692-5856fe3c1c3e">表現が被りそうな場合は、amazing⇔incredible、very good⇔excellent など言い換えます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="bfa9fd5f-28d2-4d6e-add2-edeac1a81617" id="bfa9fd5f-28d2-4d6e-add2-edeac1a81617"><strong>チャンク・接続詞</strong>：</p><ul name="ec2ac52c-dd56-48dc-bf5a-38bd89f56bd3" id="ec2ac52c-dd56-48dc-bf5a-38bd89f56bd3"><li><p name="2d405a70-fcba-47e4-9562-b5c025271bd7" id="2d405a70-fcba-47e4-9562-b5c025271bd7">One of the most memorable ... was ...,</p></li><li><p name="3d0788e5-0e2a-4175-82e2-a7ff0a603388" id="3d0788e5-0e2a-4175-82e2-a7ff0a603388">What made it special was...,</p></li><li><p name="1715ea23-e5fd-486f-9085-b023396fb126" id="1715ea23-e5fd-486f-9085-b023396fb126">As a result, In addition,</p></li><li><p name="13f6ec63-04ae-4628-aede-e0b2ed7d6dd3" id="13f6ec63-04ae-4628-aede-e0b2ed7d6dd3">Because of that などを活用し、物語調に一貫性を持たせます。</p><ul name="56f775da-b7e5-4039-8baa-4e730634fa15" id="56f775da-b7e5-4039-8baa-4e730634fa15"><li><p name="47592e9a-0e3c-4fe6-ac81-a0687ef2b250" id="47592e9a-0e3c-4fe6-ac81-a0687ef2b250">言い出しに Well, I suppose ... などを軽く使って考える時間を稼ぐのも有効です。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul><p name="0ecea334-dfb2-4e31-8082-e7c891643577" id="0ecea334-dfb2-4e31-8082-e7c891643577">以下では、より詳細に12のジャンル別で実際の設問例と模範回答を示し、それぞれ語彙や構成上のポイントを解説します。</p><hr><h3 name="6d33f527-6829-47da-a14c-3d5843f543d2" id="6d33f527-6829-47da-a14c-3d5843f543d2">旅行(Travel)</h3><p name="17a8c692-414a-4a9a-a7df-f19687622ea0" id="17a8c692-414a-4a9a-a7df-f19687622ea0"><strong>質問例：&nbsp;</strong>“Describe a memorable trip you went on.”<br>「あなたが行った印象的な旅について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）：</strong></p><figure name="021644c0-3f6d-4d8a-ba85-03638097bafe" id="021644c0-3f6d-4d8a-ba85-03638097bafe"><blockquote><p name="6ef3c35a-06bb-4ca5-b2f2-7aaf50de605d" id="6ef3c35a-06bb-4ca5-b2f2-7aaf50de605d">Last spring I went on a weekend trip to Kyoto with my family. <br><br>We visited famous temples like Kinkaku-ji and Fushimi Inari, and the weather was perfectly sunny. <br>I remember taking many photos of the beautiful gardens. <br>We also tried traditional Japanese food, which was delicious. <br><br>During the evenings we walked along quiet streets and enjoyed the peaceful atmosphere. <br>This trip was really memorable for me because I had never traveled with my family before, and it brought us closer together. <br><br>Overall, it was a wonderful experience that I will never forget.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="6ca53312-1266-455a-9b7a-aa6c67e07db3" id="6ca53312-1266-455a-9b7a-aa6c67e07db3"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="dcdae8d2-f2d3-46c6-807b-67a88e469368" id="dcdae8d2-f2d3-46c6-807b-67a88e469368"><li><p name="8a46bd6c-4a44-4aa6-b81f-9c6a0338d4db" id="8a46bd6c-4a44-4aa6-b81f-9c6a0338d4db"><strong>5W1Hで構成：</strong></p><ul name="fb2158c3-4c9e-4c0c-bcbf-299b37694740" id="fb2158c3-4c9e-4c0c-bcbf-299b37694740"><li><p name="efd2a5bd-c2cb-42e8-bcf0-a773d64de007" id="efd2a5bd-c2cb-42e8-bcf0-a773d64de007"><strong>&nbsp;</strong>「いつ (When)：Last spring（昨春）に」</p></li><li><p name="ae9c21c1-124e-4492-b167-6b2c1ae9b250" id="ae9c21c1-124e-4492-b167-6b2c1ae9b250">「どこで (Where)：京都へ」</p></li><li><p name="8ed74b1e-e929-4901-b06f-a897ffab3435" id="8ed74b1e-e929-4901-b06f-a897ffab3435">「誰と (Who)：家族と」</p></li><li><p name="16f90dc3-100a-4bf8-8775-6fe2627018e5" id="16f90dc3-100a-4bf8-8775-6fe2627018e5">「何をした (What)：お寺を観光し、写真を撮り、日本食を試した」</p></li><li><p name="5e34fdc1-13f5-4e82-8c1f-f2148f22770b" id="5e34fdc1-13f5-4e82-8c1f-f2148f22770b">「なぜ特別か (Why)：家族旅行が初めてで絆が深まったから」…といった情報を時系列でカバーしています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="f6338596-51e8-405a-a191-20dbc095298b" id="f6338596-51e8-405a-a191-20dbc095298b"><strong>時系列展開：</strong></p><ul name="713f3064-80ce-4461-8fca-f8e2f848f959" id="713f3064-80ce-4461-8fca-f8e2f848f959"><li><p name="771bb9a2-b4a8-4026-bc07-6c573ce6c548" id="771bb9a2-b4a8-4026-bc07-6c573ce6c548">最初に過去形で旅行の始まりを説明し（Last spring）</p></li><li><p name="c5b50eb0-e33c-4f8e-b882-0ea32c2396f0" id="c5b50eb0-e33c-4f8e-b882-0ea32c2396f0">次に行程（visited, tried）を詳細に述べ</p></li><li><p name="b6899206-8351-4a13-90b4-57dbd1782b99" id="b6899206-8351-4a13-90b4-57dbd1782b99">最後に「This trip was really memorable...」でまとめています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="b6b44a96-789a-4f36-be90-0aa71f23d1fc" id="b6b44a96-789a-4f36-be90-0aa71f23d1fc"><strong>語彙・表現：</strong></p><ul name="637e3ed7-6846-42a4-ad41-49df9455ef98" id="637e3ed7-6846-42a4-ad41-49df9455ef98"><li><p name="404db592-d109-4bca-ba6f-10e05cf8a22c" id="404db592-d109-4bca-ba6f-10e05cf8a22c">memorable（忘れられない）</p></li><li><p name="2a23aa37-022f-46cf-8167-8993e44d6ac0" id="2a23aa37-022f-46cf-8167-8993e44d6ac0">famous temples（有名な寺院）</p></li><li><p name="734bad90-6e19-4e41-b1f0-85bd0036a69b" id="734bad90-6e19-4e41-b1f0-85bd0036a69b">traditional（伝統的な）</p></li><li><p name="e0720c58-f715-4153-a8d8-ced83f56e510" id="e0720c58-f715-4153-a8d8-ced83f56e510">peaceful atmosphere（穏やかな雰囲気）など、旅行の描写にふさわしい語彙を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="c9d98c3a-72b2-4c1a-843b-35bcdac01b4d" id="c9d98c3a-72b2-4c1a-843b-35bcdac01b4d"><strong>結論：</strong></p><ul name="66247cee-e87b-4b08-8a86-ef5fa54127be" id="66247cee-e87b-4b08-8a86-ef5fa54127be"><li><p name="6e8b9966-984c-43b5-b751-9323577cced2" id="6e8b9966-984c-43b5-b751-9323577cced2">「Overall, it was a wonderful experience...」で自分の感情や総括を述べ、締めくくっています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="f6328b6b-463e-4b94-8d0a-1a560dec140b" id="f6328b6b-463e-4b94-8d0a-1a560dec140b">人物 (Person)</h3><p name="c25ecbf6-31bc-4ddf-8d77-28e409a00369" id="c25ecbf6-31bc-4ddf-8d77-28e409a00369"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a family member you are closest to.”<br>「あなたが一番親しい家族について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="0f0b9051-60c4-4213-88de-a236e9fda671" id="0f0b9051-60c4-4213-88de-a236e9fda671"><blockquote><p name="0c1d1419-b2e8-49e7-b37d-ad0d4c93fb88" id="0c1d1419-b2e8-49e7-b37d-ad0d4c93fb88">I’d like to talk about my older sister, who is the person I am closest to. <br><br>She is four years older than me, and we grew up together in the same house. <br>Ever since I was a child, she always helped me with my homework and taught me new things. <br>For example, when I struggled with math in school, she patiently explained it to me after dinner. <br><br>We also share many hobbies: we often cook together on weekends and watch movies in the evenings. <br>My sister is very kind and understanding, and I can always talk to her about anything. <br>Because she cares about me and supports me, I really admire and trust her. <br><br>In conclusion, she’s not only my sister but also my best friend, and I’m grateful to have her in my life.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="04a54bc6-6bcb-482a-bfbb-530dc160dbb5" id="04a54bc6-6bcb-482a-bfbb-530dc160dbb5"><strong>解説:</strong></p><ul name="23458717-64bc-4744-ab51-d638152a0979" id="23458717-64bc-4744-ab51-d638152a0979"><li><p name="352ec5a8-e245-438e-8784-0272ffc800d3" id="352ec5a8-e245-438e-8784-0272ffc800d3"><strong>Who・How：</strong></p><ul name="cdc65d2e-6cf7-4a55-b133-c8a1639c5a07" id="cdc65d2e-6cf7-4a55-b133-c8a1639c5a07"><li><p name="f6619456-598b-4c1b-bdfa-cc41f35ab2ed" id="f6619456-598b-4c1b-bdfa-cc41f35ab2ed">「Who： older sister（姉）」</p></li><li><p name="09c287ed-0578-4806-b865-ab6e7d726843" id="09c287ed-0578-4806-b865-ab6e7d726843">「How：grew up together」など、自己紹介＋関係性を明示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="98e86a79-823e-4444-8f52-b5452400e512" id="98e86a79-823e-4444-8f52-b5452400e512"><strong>具体例：</strong></p><ul name="851315b4-86db-47d3-a2b5-4b8a9007edf7" id="851315b4-86db-47d3-a2b5-4b8a9007edf7"><li><p name="96fb0091-f521-445e-9262-51e3154d1b43" id="96fb0091-f521-445e-9262-51e3154d1b43">「数学の宿題を教えてくれた」「一緒に料理や映画鑑賞」など具体的エピソードで姉との絆を示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="442e479a-1f30-41fb-add6-c272733ef286" id="442e479a-1f30-41fb-add6-c272733ef286"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="f54d6487-f6aa-41b8-bc8f-1f1cba88b61b" id="f54d6487-f6aa-41b8-bc8f-1f1cba88b61b"><li><p name="362d121d-01e1-48e7-9a90-c68c30109770" id="362d121d-01e1-48e7-9a90-c68c30109770">admire（尊敬する）</p></li><li><p name="4b6e030e-c082-4593-a483-d74226a85d36" id="4b6e030e-c082-4593-a483-d74226a85d36">trust（信頼する）</p></li><li><p name="ff3bead9-64a9-4a49-923e-39169072c42d" id="ff3bead9-64a9-4a49-923e-39169072c42d">patiently（忍耐強く）</p></li><li><p name="e351020e-29c2-4ea6-b231-252aba408c8e" id="e351020e-29c2-4ea6-b231-252aba408c8e">share hobbies（趣味を共有する）といった表現で好意的な印象を与えています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="2f70da96-0af8-441f-89c2-8845a093f745" id="2f70da96-0af8-441f-89c2-8845a093f745"><strong>感情表現：</strong></p><ul name="82e9180a-4746-4642-bc9d-bb6ed5a0ec5e" id="82e9180a-4746-4642-bc9d-bb6ed5a0ec5e"><li><p name="a138abd4-e716-483d-a116-b52e12ba6eef" id="a138abd4-e716-483d-a116-b52e12ba6eef">I really admire and trust her（私は本当に尊敬し信頼しています）と感謝の気持ちを伝え、終わりにbest friend（親友）の言葉で締めています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="3419e85d-2924-469f-a365-3ccacb3431b0" id="3419e85d-2924-469f-a365-3ccacb3431b0">動物 (Animal)</h3><p name="faf48856-97d6-4a70-8291-51afa2c63d15" id="faf48856-97d6-4a70-8291-51afa2c63d15"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a time when you saw an interesting animal.”<br>「面白い動物を見たときについて説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）：</strong></p><figure name="c257131d-5443-4270-9a0e-728d28d507c0" id="c257131d-5443-4270-9a0e-728d28d507c0"><blockquote><p name="66623d39-72f7-46d4-bf16-9b42ffa0b62e" id="66623d39-72f7-46d4-bf16-9b42ffa0b62e">Last autumn I visited Nara Park in Japan, which is famous for its deer. <br><br>One morning I saw a particularly large deer near a shrine. <br>It was calmly eating grass and seemed completely unafraid of people. <br>I had some crackers in my hand, and to my surprise the deer gently took one from me.<br><br>We stood still together for a while; the deer looking at me with big, dark eyes. <br>I felt really excited and a bit nervous because wild animals are usually shy, but this one was very friendly. <br>Seeing such a gentle animal up close was a memorable moment. <br><br>In conclusion, that encounter with the deer was special because it was so peaceful and unexpected.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="128d01ab-bf9b-4d5e-91b7-85fe653e6985" id="128d01ab-bf9b-4d5e-91b7-85fe653e6985"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="e2295fd8-d82f-4c92-810f-5890a7718805" id="e2295fd8-d82f-4c92-810f-5890a7718805"><li><p name="609125a6-f19a-4547-a099-ad6a4e692e41" id="609125a6-f19a-4547-a099-ad6a4e692e41"><strong>Where・What：</strong></p><ul name="1ae3dc44-4b4f-4b6e-9faf-0f9a557f47da" id="1ae3dc44-4b4f-4b6e-9faf-0f9a557f47da"><li><p name="79b0e2fa-733d-4305-bcf0-6e64dbbc24f8" id="79b0e2fa-733d-4305-bcf0-6e64dbbc24f8">「場所：奈良公園」</p></li><li><p name="6dd129ef-3ae4-4cab-984d-05ec738729f1" id="6dd129ef-3ae4-4cab-984d-05ec738729f1">「動物：大きな鹿」と具体的に設定しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="fbd89ca9-b76d-4aa5-9f11-26b9c02faf8a" id="fbd89ca9-b76d-4aa5-9f11-26b9c02faf8a"><strong>状況説明：</strong></p><ul name="6cc99e9e-6e30-438e-99ba-4aed3f494f1d" id="6cc99e9e-6e30-438e-99ba-4aed3f494f1d"><li><p name="933d5f0b-f9ac-4e2e-a775-3d6f047b827e" id="933d5f0b-f9ac-4e2e-a775-3d6f047b827e">eating grass, gently took one from me のような描写でその場面を生き生きと再現しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="4bdd8003-72c2-48f6-90ab-a1f26baeda20" id="4bdd8003-72c2-48f6-90ab-a1f26baeda20"><strong>感情表現</strong></p><ul name="640b358d-7974-4401-a263-148cbbd406c0" id="640b358d-7974-4401-a263-148cbbd406c0"><li><p name="af436048-9bda-4725-9272-a5283a6e44f2" id="af436048-9bda-4725-9272-a5283a6e44f2">really excited and a bit nervous（本当に興奮し、少し緊張していた）と自分の気持ちを交えています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="d85807ef-290e-41ec-9891-c5822ff140e1" id="d85807ef-290e-41ec-9891-c5822ff140e1"><strong>結論</strong></p><ul name="ede11e5f-b3d8-433c-b56a-c50dc2bd8a49" id="ede11e5f-b3d8-433c-b56a-c50dc2bd8a49"><li><p name="a7ebcc14-e323-4e8f-8dce-ebdb0212f5a8" id="a7ebcc14-e323-4e8f-8dce-ebdb0212f5a8">That encounter with the deer was special（鹿との出会いは特別だった）で、なぜ興味深かったかをまとめています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="99b02e0f-a677-4941-903f-92dfc17c37c0" id="99b02e0f-a677-4941-903f-92dfc17c37c0"><strong>語彙</strong></p><ul name="e9f48380-8cbd-43f9-bf76-6aabb8424808" id="e9f48380-8cbd-43f9-bf76-6aabb8424808"><li><p name="a01b0ab6-538f-46f9-ac9a-7812c3757366" id="a01b0ab6-538f-46f9-ac9a-7812c3757366">shy（おとなしい）</p></li><li><p name="3ff33b16-ce4d-4858-a3ea-00b0f2dd561c" id="3ff33b16-ce4d-4858-a3ea-00b0f2dd561c">friendly（人懐っこい）</p></li><li><p name="1c0771c5-64c8-4e77-9172-34cef1d9b6ff" id="1c0771c5-64c8-4e77-9172-34cef1d9b6ff">gentle（優しい）など動物の性格を表す表現を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="a72fe831-044e-4b37-9110-9398c245237c" id="a72fe831-044e-4b37-9110-9398c245237c">建物 (Building)</h3><p name="1f82eaf4-7cdf-400c-ad54-e2b55c3bec5d" id="1f82eaf4-7cdf-400c-ad54-e2b55c3bec5d"><strong>質問例：<br></strong>“Describe a tall building in your hometown you like or dislike.”<br>「あなたの地元にある高い建物で、好きまたは嫌いなものについて説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）：</strong></p><figure name="813edc82-987f-404f-acc2-ddeadf083a07" id="813edc82-987f-404f-acc2-ddeadf083a07"><blockquote><p name="f49946ba-caac-4c07-a3b7-e8c1fc659bdc" id="f49946ba-caac-4c07-a3b7-e8c1fc659bdc">In my hometown there is a tall skyscraper called “Sunshine Tower” that I really like. <br><br>It was built about ten years ago and stands 50 stories high. <br>I usually see it on my way to work every morning. <br>The building has a modern design with a glass facade that reflects the sky. <br><br>At night, it lights up with colorful patterns. <br>I like this building because it makes the city look vibrant and modern.<br>Walking past it always feels impressive. <br>In contrast, there is also an old abandoned building nearby that I dislike because it looks neglected. <br>But Sunshine Tower is well-maintained and symbolizes progress to me. <br><br>In conclusion, its impressive height and design make it a favorite landmark of mine.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="2a842133-a958-40c4-9d58-b8cb82e5b3c3" id="2a842133-a958-40c4-9d58-b8cb82e5b3c3"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="a41263b7-7f64-4e2d-a395-da8b91ad8dcb" id="a41263b7-7f64-4e2d-a395-da8b91ad8dcb"><li><p name="98d160a7-02da-40c8-8820-e4e488530611" id="98d160a7-02da-40c8-8820-e4e488530611"><strong>外観描写：</strong></p><ul name="1affd955-4d11-4daf-bab2-3dd6f7081d48" id="1affd955-4d11-4daf-bab2-3dd6f7081d48"><li><p name="5bf17784-24f7-4289-8ce7-ce2b4b361c00" id="5bf17784-24f7-4289-8ce7-ce2b4b361c00">50 stories high（50階建て）</p></li><li><p name="db6b71d5-0a48-4488-9ba3-6f1859fdc142" id="db6b71d5-0a48-4488-9ba3-6f1859fdc142">glass facade that reflects the sky（空を映すガラス張りの外観）</p></li><li><p name="3cac72a7-1085-4849-82db-72b104646c7c" id="3cac72a7-1085-4849-82db-72b104646c7c">lights up with colorful patterns（カラフルな光でライトアップされる）など具体的に説明しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="4eac2d07-08fc-4e50-aba9-260732e9f46a" id="4eac2d07-08fc-4e50-aba9-260732e9f46a"><strong>位置・状況：</strong></p><ul name="1196d943-592c-4134-ba44-a92eb35f6596" id="1196d943-592c-4134-ba44-a92eb35f6596"><li><p name="0efae63a-8f7a-4b88-aadc-14cd1ec6cf89" id="0efae63a-8f7a-4b88-aadc-14cd1ec6cf89">on my way to work every morning（毎朝通勤で見かける）と日常の様子を述べています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a0bcd2e6-ae12-45f4-ae74-b940a627546a" id="a0bcd2e6-ae12-45f4-ae74-b940a627546a"><strong>比較：</strong></p><ul name="d80883aa-bebb-4892-b6aa-6f5869e9fc75" id="d80883aa-bebb-4892-b6aa-6f5869e9fc75"><li><p name="62c061bd-a71a-480e-9e51-452d1bd3c047" id="62c061bd-a71a-480e-9e51-452d1bd3c047">良い例（Sunshine Tower）と悪い例（廃墟ビル）を対比させ、Towerへの好感を強調しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="98574861-78df-4f5c-b646-f81bf4b0c7fc" id="98574861-78df-4f5c-b646-f81bf4b0c7fc"><strong>感想：</strong></p><ul name="ddceb788-7aeb-49d1-82a3-005ee9a1f711" id="ddceb788-7aeb-49d1-82a3-005ee9a1f711"><li><p name="f1bd177b-1389-44da-9efe-6241aa5acff4" id="f1bd177b-1389-44da-9efe-6241aa5acff4">impressive height and design make it a favorite landmark（その堂々たる高さとデザインはお気に入りの名所です）と結論づけています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="69b32de8-5d50-4b0e-940a-84bee50fb0d5" id="69b32de8-5d50-4b0e-940a-84bee50fb0d5">広告 (Advertisement)</h3><p name="af96320e-fe46-4b83-8de8-65291d0500e9" id="af96320e-fe46-4b83-8de8-65291d0500e9"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe an advertisement you have seen/heard recently.”<br>「最近見たり聞いたりした広告について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）：</strong></p><figure name="b9e48903-ac5d-4899-9fae-52e9f11d05c0" id="b9e48903-ac5d-4899-9fae-52e9f11d05c0"><blockquote><p name="14bee546-1905-4d54-b37c-5f7411bb0ebd" id="14bee546-1905-4d54-b37c-5f7411bb0ebd">Recently I saw a TV commercial for a new smartphone model. <br><br>It aired last month during a popular evening show. <br>In the advertisement, a famous actor holds the phone while highlighting its features: a high-quality camera, long battery life, and a fast processor.<br>The background music was upbeat and the visuals were very colorful. <br><br>I felt impressed because the phone looked sleek and powerful. <br>However, the ad didn’t mention the price, which made me curious. <br>I liked the commercial overall because it showed how handy the phone can be in everyday life. <br><br>In conclusion, it’s a compelling ad that makes me interested in the product.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="0fc1965f-fc59-44de-a699-3138796e5b5f" id="0fc1965f-fc59-44de-a699-3138796e5b5f"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="dbe2d944-a5c6-4c44-bd0d-507537c59353" id="dbe2d944-a5c6-4c44-bd0d-507537c59353"><li><p name="85f3c060-9590-4c54-bc9e-a30e4e9fe95f" id="85f3c060-9590-4c54-bc9e-a30e4e9fe95f"><strong>When/What：</strong></p><ul name="47146f1b-9dde-4319-bd5a-72c1adc4ae18" id="47146f1b-9dde-4319-bd5a-72c1adc4ae18"><li><p name="90b9e5e1-dca7-4e19-b242-a3110255b292" id="90b9e5e1-dca7-4e19-b242-a3110255b292">last month during a popular evening show（先月の人気番組中に）</p></li><li><p name="d5c30f49-e10c-4129-a8c6-77eeffb96e67" id="d5c30f49-e10c-4129-a8c6-77eeffb96e67">new smartphone model（新型スマホ）など時期と内容を説明しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="5a7c9fef-1433-4a31-9109-630be11b4f83" id="5a7c9fef-1433-4a31-9109-630be11b4f83"><strong>内容：</strong></p><ul name="3874ea99-22d0-4387-9a65-3b367787b2b2" id="3874ea99-22d0-4387-9a65-3b367787b2b2"><li><p name="9ad1de21-340d-4b50-8b56-215634633f74" id="9ad1de21-340d-4b50-8b56-215634633f74">high-quality camera, long battery life, fast processor（高性能カメラ、長いバッテリー持続時間、高速プロセッサー）と、広告で強調された特徴を列挙しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a1c2fcc3-fc2e-49e5-9b67-97a0486334a9" id="a1c2fcc3-fc2e-49e5-9b67-97a0486334a9"><strong>感想：</strong></p><ul name="3d306b95-9578-4c81-8ebb-e7973cc77643" id="3d306b95-9578-4c81-8ebb-e7973cc77643"><li><p name="075270fa-c167-490f-8950-62a97ccbe1eb" id="075270fa-c167-490f-8950-62a97ccbe1eb">I felt impressed（感銘を受けた）</p></li><li><p name="fe0a7059-84bf-4d3f-a764-f59ba146cc7c" id="fe0a7059-84bf-4d3f-a764-f59ba146cc7c">compelling（魅力的な）など、広告への評価を述べています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="ebbff46d-de78-4390-a93f-b7e2227e2e94" id="ebbff46d-de78-4390-a93f-b7e2227e2e94"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="b4c2e7b0-68fe-4e3b-aeac-20d5bb0759d2" id="b4c2e7b0-68fe-4e3b-aeac-20d5bb0759d2"><li><p name="8139a459-fde4-42d9-8490-5121cb775cc3" id="8139a459-fde4-42d9-8490-5121cb775cc3">sleek（洗練された）</p></li><li><p name="5e4c1496-c923-421b-901a-1013912b7faf" id="5e4c1496-c923-421b-901a-1013912b7faf">upbeat（陽気な）など広告の雰囲気を表す単語を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="45d827c7-96c3-45cb-bb0d-b5290105f323" id="45d827c7-96c3-45cb-bb0d-b5290105f323">本 (Book)</h3><p name="83b6ef76-e361-4ef2-988f-7500ae2c342f" id="83b6ef76-e361-4ef2-988f-7500ae2c342f"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a story or novel you have recently read that you found particularly interesting.”<br>「最近読んで興味深かった物語や小説について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="1d5ec18e-eca3-48de-9aaa-9648e8531d8d" id="1d5ec18e-eca3-48de-9aaa-9648e8531d8d"><blockquote><p name="9885dfa8-664b-404d-8940-4f2fc5da3d99" id="9885dfa8-664b-404d-8940-4f2fc5da3d99">I recently read “The Alchemist” by Paulo Coelho, which is a novel about a young shepherd’s journey. <br><br>The story follows the shepherd, Santiago, as he travels across the desert to find treasure in Egypt. <br>Along the way, he meets various people—like a king, a crystal merchant, and an alchemist—who teach him important life lessons.<br><br>The book is rich in philosophical ideas and metaphors. <br>I found it fascinating because it talks about following your dreams and listening to your heart. <br>I enjoyed the writing style, which is simple yet meaningful. <br><br>In conclusion, “The Alchemist” was particularly interesting because it inspired me to pursue my own goals and view life as an adventure.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="901a9f9b-dda0-4ff3-8f34-2d120e36feea" id="901a9f9b-dda0-4ff3-8f34-2d120e36feea"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="70d59c1e-5c67-4786-8dd9-3f19d6a6467e" id="70d59c1e-5c67-4786-8dd9-3f19d6a6467e"><li><p name="67abbb55-0912-4316-8b3d-cdc9e6e5fbd1" id="67abbb55-0912-4316-8b3d-cdc9e6e5fbd1"><strong>あらすじ：</strong></p><ul name="04898bba-bf19-4bfa-8d3b-fb671bb285fb" id="04898bba-bf19-4bfa-8d3b-fb671bb285fb"><li><p name="4c294659-4c75-49cf-ab50-e58b7c4e225f" id="4c294659-4c75-49cf-ab50-e58b7c4e225f">a young shepherd’s journey（若い羊飼いの旅）や登場人物（王様や錬金術師）などを簡潔に要約しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="05b26c2c-d665-418c-b869-40b9727441bc" id="05b26c2c-d665-418c-b869-40b9727441bc"><strong>感想：</strong></p><ul name="adc0d9ea-93ce-496c-ac51-cc6db319e462" id="adc0d9ea-93ce-496c-ac51-cc6db319e462"><li><p name="35ebeed0-3db4-450f-996f-fdb3f1ecb524" id="35ebeed0-3db4-450f-996f-fdb3f1ecb524">fascinating（魅力的な）</p></li><li><p name="13b4e8d4-a11f-443d-bef7-93cd0bd09ef5" id="13b4e8d4-a11f-443d-bef7-93cd0bd09ef5">inspired me（私に刺激を与えた）など、物語が与えた影響を述べています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="20dd7dbe-e09d-4fbe-a6db-29f3f505b0df" id="20dd7dbe-e09d-4fbe-a6db-29f3f505b0df"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="079e0fb2-0aea-4fcb-904e-040cb6821cd9" id="079e0fb2-0aea-4fcb-904e-040cb6821cd9"><li><p name="21a61420-8c18-4405-a848-3a62b5289d1b" id="21a61420-8c18-4405-a848-3a62b5289d1b">philosophical ideas（哲学的な考え）</p></li><li><p name="5361662d-b59b-40af-97a0-98da68cb914a" id="5361662d-b59b-40af-97a0-98da68cb914a">metaphors（比喩）</p></li><li><p name="4d99ccfd-bd5e-4def-826f-0b779aa54e49" id="4d99ccfd-bd5e-4def-826f-0b779aa54e49">writing style（文体）など、本の特徴を表す語彙を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="84f6ed20-1624-4914-bcfc-b3ed9c775412" id="84f6ed20-1624-4914-bcfc-b3ed9c775412"><strong>結論：</strong></p><ul name="64b3bd6e-d692-44e3-be4c-4d85b2f380a6" id="64b3bd6e-d692-44e3-be4c-4d85b2f380a6"><li><p name="67210e4e-1049-4d39-897f-cc56513e799b" id="67210e4e-1049-4d39-897f-cc56513e799b">inspired me to pursue my own goals（自分の目標を追いかけるように刺激された）と、自分への影響で締めくくっています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="0014c7e6-f72f-4feb-9ccb-2fb9d7600522" id="0014c7e6-f72f-4feb-9ccb-2fb9d7600522">会話 (Conversation)</h3><p name="d25addf1-2f7e-4f99-969b-c122dba34549" id="d25addf1-2f7e-4f99-969b-c122dba34549"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe an interesting conversation you had with someone you did not know.”<br>「知らない人との印象的な会話について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="6a712326-a0ea-44fc-b498-5f715dbd5e37" id="6a712326-a0ea-44fc-b498-5f715dbd5e37"><blockquote><p name="60bf3f57-aa3e-4d02-b1bb-b82946e6411e" id="60bf3f57-aa3e-4d02-b1bb-b82946e6411e">A few months ago, I was on a train heading home when I struck up a conversation with a stranger sitting next to me. <br><br>He was a man in his fifties, and I was reading a book. <br>He noticed the book and asked me about it. <br>We then talked about our favorite novels and authors. <br><br>After that, we discussed cultural differences in reading habits. <br>He shared that he prefers newspapers, while I enjoy fiction. <br>I found this conversation interesting because despite our age gap, we discovered a shared love of stories. <br>It lasted for almost 20 minutes and was very friendly. <br><br>In conclusion, talking to him was fascinating and showed me that people from different generations can connect through common interests.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="e25fd452-d41e-458a-86d4-0801a0373ee5" id="e25fd452-d41e-458a-86d4-0801a0373ee5"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="db09f27d-8f29-44df-bb98-414eedfb3680" id="db09f27d-8f29-44df-bb98-414eedfb3680"><li><p name="5b402e3c-0155-4f7f-a7f0-71c949ea05e8" id="5b402e3c-0155-4f7f-a7f0-71c949ea05e8"><strong>場面設定：</strong></p><ul name="0b1bbce2-348d-4c11-ab00-1ed2dd146204" id="0b1bbce2-348d-4c11-ab00-1ed2dd146204"><li><p name="26f73080-1ab4-43c6-870f-442de05a4f46" id="26f73080-1ab4-43c6-870f-442de05a4f46">on a train heading home（帰宅途中の電車内）</p></li><li><p name="cb6cb26a-73fb-4f77-9ae6-d9205353ccaf" id="cb6cb26a-73fb-4f77-9ae6-d9205353ccaf">stranger sitting next to me（隣の知らない人）と状況を説明しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a7fa2f72-9446-49c4-947c-4eb935271df4" id="a7fa2f72-9446-49c4-947c-4eb935271df4"><strong>話題：</strong></p><ul name="20408931-6e43-43f0-ae04-e185a016867a" id="20408931-6e43-43f0-ae04-e185a016867a"><li><p name="f7d56f49-be8d-4f4e-b78a-53174613ce0d" id="f7d56f49-be8d-4f4e-b78a-53174613ce0d">favorite novels and authors（好きな小説や作家）</p></li><li><p name="28f213fb-d922-45ff-bdee-1e59e6dcb793" id="28f213fb-d922-45ff-bdee-1e59e6dcb793">cultural differences in reading habits（読書習慣の文化的違い）などを会話の内容として述べています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="31ad27da-242d-4b00-9f8e-fb08cd049222" id="31ad27da-242d-4b00-9f8e-fb08cd049222"><strong>感想：</strong></p><ul name="0ef16280-a080-4abb-bffd-724427fb7503" id="0ef16280-a080-4abb-bffd-724427fb7503"><li><p name="6b5842f7-bea0-4060-92af-2a5af0727d9c" id="6b5842f7-bea0-4060-92af-2a5af0727d9c">I found this conversation interesting（この会話は興味深かった）</p></li><li><p name="9ce30c5c-02a9-4e04-80b6-de9c8a717a8e" id="9ce30c5c-02a9-4e04-80b6-de9c8a717a8e">fascinating（魅力的だった）と自己の感情を表現しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a24ae600-2fde-468f-b15f-2610a2754637" id="a24ae600-2fde-468f-b15f-2610a2754637"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="a2f875fd-3ec1-4986-ac6c-3b9bfa38f312" id="a2f875fd-3ec1-4986-ac6c-3b9bfa38f312"><li><p name="af0d5ab0-8994-453d-be36-b03bcd5d3403" id="af0d5ab0-8994-453d-be36-b03bcd5d3403">struck up a conversation（会話を始める）</p></li><li><p name="f709f448-462a-4910-be3d-079c56b7f012" id="f709f448-462a-4910-be3d-079c56b7f012">age gap（年齢差）</p></li><li><p name="c219983f-acdd-4d2a-83b1-36c9ebd2dd72" id="c219983f-acdd-4d2a-83b1-36c9ebd2dd72">shared love of stories（物語への共通の愛好）などの表現を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="28382221-4324-4916-b650-b34c4cd394e1" id="28382221-4324-4916-b650-b34c4cd394e1">決断 (Decision)</h3><p name="fd957ee0-cdc7-4a28-8063-9a789f3df70f" id="fd957ee0-cdc7-4a28-8063-9a789f3df70f"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a difficult decision that you made.”<br>「あなたが下した難しい決断について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="0e0af252-933e-4859-9a2e-7e55d5b5b8ce" id="0e0af252-933e-4859-9a2e-7e55d5b5b8ce"><blockquote><p name="b2d3c027-2645-4602-9bdf-1795c975c809" id="b2d3c027-2645-4602-9bdf-1795c975c809">About a year ago, I faced a difficult decision: whether to move to another city for a job offer. <br><br>I had been offered a position at a company in Osaka, but it meant leaving my hometown Tokyo and my friends and family behind. <br>The decision was hard because the job was a great opportunity, but I also valued my current life. <br><br>I spent the weekend weighing the pros and cons: better career prospects versus being far from loved ones. <br>I talked with my family and friends to get advice. <br>In the end, I decided to accept the job. <br>It was challenging at first, but I believe it helped me grow professionally and personally. <br><br>In conclusion, making this decision was difficult because it involved balancing my career goals with my personal life.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="95564f6b-bc87-4e6d-8a71-f55d599fc171" id="95564f6b-bc87-4e6d-8a71-f55d599fc171"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="952df088-e5b3-4172-bc58-accebfd59833" id="952df088-e5b3-4172-bc58-accebfd59833"><li><p name="ab37a8fe-d717-4b4d-b3bf-89e52a415432" id="ab37a8fe-d717-4b4d-b3bf-89e52a415432"><strong>問題点：</strong></p><ul name="d36737ca-4870-45eb-9ae0-93af0b43e950" id="d36737ca-4870-45eb-9ae0-93af0b43e950"><li><p name="55a044ca-a132-4a6b-9078-f9f53b634098" id="55a044ca-a132-4a6b-9078-f9f53b634098">Osakaに移るか、今の生活を維持するかというジレンマを具体的に述べています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="43d695b5-fc0f-4718-a994-42092be7f590" id="43d695b5-fc0f-4718-a994-42092be7f590"><strong>対策：</strong></p><ul name="0863442f-6560-4ee5-94f2-bec04220c0d3" id="0863442f-6560-4ee5-94f2-bec04220c0d3"><li><p name="83cbe0c2-07fc-40d8-9924-58fd380e78d1" id="83cbe0c2-07fc-40d8-9924-58fd380e78d1">weekend weighing the pros and cons（週末に利点と欠点を天秤にかけた）</p></li><li><p name="6c73bcfe-4cf5-478e-989d-b6a085fe3392" id="6c73bcfe-4cf5-478e-989d-b6a085fe3392">talked with my family（家族と話した）など、検討プロセスを示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="da2bd380-a4df-41fd-8804-6009173d3c73" id="da2bd380-a4df-41fd-8804-6009173d3c73"><strong>感情</strong>：</p><ul name="6eac1f96-920c-42e9-996d-c2b3670f63a1" id="6eac1f96-920c-42e9-996d-c2b3670f63a1"><li><p name="376d6cc9-beed-43c6-a853-b329cb630642" id="376d6cc9-beed-43c6-a853-b329cb630642">difficult decision（難しい決断）</p></li><li><p name="f64269b8-ceac-425d-9d66-c1d6b7a62f93" id="f64269b8-ceac-425d-9d66-c1d6b7a62f93">challenging at first（最初は大変だった）と気持ちの変化を含めています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="deaf5bf2-4b74-40ec-975c-7d08c1ea9ad0" id="deaf5bf2-4b74-40ec-975c-7d08c1ea9ad0"><strong>結論：</strong></p><ul name="f54bbdac-ce47-4dec-b82c-41c406ba8cc5" id="f54bbdac-ce47-4dec-b82c-41c406ba8cc5"><li><p name="82139b0e-4fa0-4edd-992a-558718fb456a" id="82139b0e-4fa0-4edd-992a-558718fb456a">balancing my career goals with my personal life（仕事の目標と私生活の両立）に触れ、なぜ難しかったかをまとめています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="c99d9f43-39c3-420d-a0d6-38add9213bdb" id="c99d9f43-39c3-420d-a0d6-38add9213bdb">学校 (School)</h3><p name="65ae5440-e40f-4d6b-992b-148b3a93e226" id="65ae5440-e40f-4d6b-992b-148b3a93e226"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a teacher who has influenced you in your education.”<br>「あなたの教育に影響を与えた先生について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）：</strong></p><figure name="3bbc2dbc-5778-4f45-9217-4d8bcbcc67ac" id="3bbc2dbc-5778-4f45-9217-4d8bcbcc67ac"><blockquote><p name="63492630-8198-4993-b80d-0b030d71dc39" id="63492630-8198-4993-b80d-0b030d71dc39">I’d like to talk about my high school math teacher, Mr. Tanaka. <br><br>I first met him when I was a sophomore. <br>He taught algebra and geometry. <br><br>What was special about him was his unique teaching style. <br>He made complex concepts very simple. <br>For example, he used real-life examples to explain equations, so we could easily understand abstract ideas. <br><br>He was also very patient and always encouraged questions. <br>Because of him, I started to enjoy math and my grades improved significantly. <br><br>In conclusion, Mr. Tanaka influenced me greatly by making me confident in math and showing me the importance of patience in learning.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="a647acc6-7c38-41e5-93b4-4f3afb2ff0e6" id="a647acc6-7c38-41e5-93b4-4f3afb2ff0e6"><strong>解説:</strong></p><ul name="0c4d4e18-a80c-448c-8e8a-975fc414e879" id="0c4d4e18-a80c-448c-8e8a-975fc414e879"><li><p name="ca2acf44-c499-4909-b395-09d7517dc933" id="ca2acf44-c499-4909-b395-09d7517dc933"><strong>出会い：</strong></p><ul name="437cc8fe-594e-4fda-8a28-5d01185bd102" id="437cc8fe-594e-4fda-8a28-5d01185bd102"><li><p name="ea968f14-1aa0-49b7-82c8-758fabe117ea" id="ea968f14-1aa0-49b7-82c8-758fabe117ea">sophomore in high school（高校2年生）など、教師との出会いの時期と教科を明示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="c016e9c8-962e-4fd7-b379-bc7a4ffa4ee3" id="c016e9c8-962e-4fd7-b379-bc7a4ffa4ee3"><strong>特徴：</strong></p><ul name="0dddc116-9f3b-45c2-a457-5708bba1a0a8" id="0dddc116-9f3b-45c2-a457-5708bba1a0a8"><li><p name="5cde6703-9934-40be-90e4-ae9224820807" id="5cde6703-9934-40be-90e4-ae9224820807">unique teaching style, real-life examples（実生活の例え）</p></li><li><p name="930d3524-b1ed-4e2b-a389-759d63ca9800" id="930d3524-b1ed-4e2b-a389-759d63ca9800">patient（忍耐強い）など、先生の特長を具体的に挙げています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="0d4c2d8a-612d-4a7d-bc3a-3a01b1567110" id="0d4c2d8a-612d-4a7d-bc3a-3a01b1567110"><strong>成果：</strong></p><ul name="54e4f041-acec-4437-9bb5-f456b4ab8902" id="54e4f041-acec-4437-9bb5-f456b4ab8902"><li><p name="0fb366a5-06da-4463-9dc2-d0ddcc6a39b0" id="0fb366a5-06da-4463-9dc2-d0ddcc6a39b0">started to enjoy math（数学を楽しむようになった）</p></li><li><p name="a9da7ef8-0a34-40aa-9280-672c1ff93f76" id="a9da7ef8-0a34-40aa-9280-672c1ff93f76">grades improved（成績が向上した）と先生から受けた影響を示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="c793bd9c-e0a6-4a6d-ae74-660560331878" id="c793bd9c-e0a6-4a6d-ae74-660560331878"><strong>結論：</strong></p><ul name="3b0bb801-8eba-4371-aa42-9421fb2802b1" id="3b0bb801-8eba-4371-aa42-9421fb2802b1"><li><p name="b96b6031-a2e6-417f-922b-a0ca735483d1" id="b96b6031-a2e6-417f-922b-a0ca735483d1">influenced me greatly by making me confident in math（数学に自信を持たせてくれた）と、影響の大きさをまとめています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="b5c0a770-8572-4d37-a276-9d8153151144" id="b5c0a770-8572-4d37-a276-9d8153151144">色彩 (Color)</h3><p name="528add3b-4287-4753-8ab8-4a4503fc408a" id="528add3b-4287-4753-8ab8-4a4503fc408a"><strong>質問例（独自作成）:</strong> “Describe a color that is important or special to you.”<br>「あなたにとって重要または特別な色について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="06e40cbe-e0f8-49c7-a69c-dc140e2d8760" id="06e40cbe-e0f8-49c7-a69c-dc140e2d8760"><blockquote><p name="2e0f7527-9270-4d2f-aa12-e1d6ab4ac0b1" id="2e0f7527-9270-4d2f-aa12-e1d6ab4ac0b1">My favorite color is blue. <br><br>I’ve liked blue since I was a child. <br>I first realized this when my parents painted my bedroom light blue, and I loved it. <br><br>I usually see blue in the sky and the sea, which makes me feel calm. <br>Blue reminds me of water and nature. I often wear blue clothes because it makes me feel confident and relaxed. <br><br>In the evenings, the blue light of the TV screen also feels soothing. I think I like blue so much because it is both peaceful and powerful. <br><br>In conclusion, blue is special to me because it brings comfort and a positive feeling whenever I see it.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="5938f2ad-0a1c-4ea9-a4df-288fbe72608e" id="5938f2ad-0a1c-4ea9-a4df-288fbe72608e"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="1fe5da77-b218-4606-8eac-9797d87b4159" id="1fe5da77-b218-4606-8eac-9797d87b4159"><li><p name="65b05202-f7f9-4477-b526-3947f5483302" id="65b05202-f7f9-4477-b526-3947f5483302"><strong>由来：</strong></p><ul name="3c8ada7c-0aea-4ce3-ac1b-e1ed5f243915" id="3c8ada7c-0aea-4ce3-ac1b-e1ed5f243915"><li><p name="f0b3566b-51d0-4c82-8cb8-2d33eee71234" id="f0b3566b-51d0-4c82-8cb8-2d33eee71234">painted my bedroom light blue as a child（子どもの頃、部屋を水色に塗ってもらった）で、青色への思い入れを示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="2871fc08-8c82-4f27-bade-d8b2cdefa106" id="2871fc08-8c82-4f27-bade-d8b2cdefa106"><strong>印象：</strong></p><ul name="00ac9fe3-8cc0-4f4c-8710-73235efc12b5" id="00ac9fe3-8cc0-4f4c-8710-73235efc12b5"><li><p name="53270ee6-adff-488c-abe1-2b010458adf5" id="53270ee6-adff-488c-abe1-2b010458adf5">sky and sea（空と海）</p></li><li><p name="180d74b9-386e-46c1-9693-43265c6d5ff5" id="180d74b9-386e-46c1-9693-43265c6d5ff5">calm（穏やか）</p></li><li><p name="30af20db-b1d7-4f04-ae54-84e6bda46d2b" id="30af20db-b1d7-4f04-ae54-84e6bda46d2b">confident（自信が持てる）など、青色がもたらすイメージや感情を述べています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="2f933300-5555-49b2-a045-aa101df29ab8" id="2f933300-5555-49b2-a045-aa101df29ab8"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="4d60b013-a665-4182-909f-f3ab5d212ad3" id="4d60b013-a665-4182-909f-f3ab5d212ad3"><li><p name="30adedb6-a5c7-46ac-af6f-850a7d0e7252" id="30adedb6-a5c7-46ac-af6f-850a7d0e7252">relaxed（落ち着いた）</p></li><li><p name="e119762a-8102-49c3-81e4-7c743b8d2e7d" id="e119762a-8102-49c3-81e4-7c743b8d2e7d">soothing（心地よい）といった色の効果を表す語彙を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="947dc6ad-3446-4507-a9ce-f48b7bf1ea20" id="947dc6ad-3446-4507-a9ce-f48b7bf1ea20"><strong>結論：</strong></p><ul name="7900407f-5f40-43f6-8b38-23a4ed108360" id="7900407f-5f40-43f6-8b38-23a4ed108360"><li><p name="d12d9b89-31ee-4732-821b-4c47288367c5" id="d12d9b89-31ee-4732-821b-4c47288367c5">blue brings comfort and a positive feeling（青は安心感と前向きな気持ちをもたらす）とまとめています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="8d0ab9c0-20e1-4dc9-9f7b-c4e1a234c559" id="8d0ab9c0-20e1-4dc9-9f7b-c4e1a234c559">絵画 (Painting)</h3><p name="4559e74f-45dc-4506-b653-3e03bf3ecc3a" id="4559e74f-45dc-4506-b653-3e03bf3ecc3a"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a drawing or painting that you like.”<br>「あなたが好きな絵画や図画について説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="29483e58-7eee-47cf-8362-5eca505056d2" id="29483e58-7eee-47cf-8362-5eca505056d2"><blockquote><p name="737eccc7-3db9-4279-a2bf-ab78c14e55d2" id="737eccc7-3db9-4279-a2bf-ab78c14e55d2">One painting I like is “Starry Night” by Vincent van Gogh. <br><br>It shows a swirling night sky over a small town. <br>The sky is full of vibrant blues and yellows, and the brushstrokes are very bold and visible. <br><br>I first saw this painting in a museum book and was amazed by how alive it looked. <br>What makes it special to me is the emotional depth: despite being a dark night, the painting feels full of movement and hope. <br>When I look at it, I feel calm and inspired. <br><br>In conclusion, I enjoy this painting because it’s both beautiful and meaningful, and it reminds me that there is beauty in darkness.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="f5940a02-d028-449d-9777-bf0679c2fe04" id="f5940a02-d028-449d-9777-bf0679c2fe04"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="ce995dc5-29a0-4813-9625-3f6eeb6da70a" id="ce995dc5-29a0-4813-9625-3f6eeb6da70a"><li><p name="c013690b-7e3c-4b01-ac71-c1696c0d4782" id="c013690b-7e3c-4b01-ac71-c1696c0d4782"><strong>描写：</strong></p><ul name="86c64907-4f1f-46cd-b9c1-8d84c0abc489" id="86c64907-4f1f-46cd-b9c1-8d84c0abc489"><li><p name="75bb108b-a78a-4f49-8b21-287bdf1ff6d5" id="75bb108b-a78a-4f49-8b21-287bdf1ff6d5">swirling night sky, vibrant blues and yellows, bold brushstrokes（渦巻く夜空、鮮やかな青と黄色、力強い筆遣い）と絵の様子を視覚的に説明しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="ac8c70ee-762f-4568-aac6-bfc75a17798e" id="ac8c70ee-762f-4568-aac6-bfc75a17798e"><strong>印象：</strong></p><ul name="ae18a679-4e7c-4c15-b0eb-48efa8ece140" id="ae18a679-4e7c-4c15-b0eb-48efa8ece140"><li><p name="51c564f0-18dd-4dda-beb5-09412a3609ca" id="51c564f0-18dd-4dda-beb5-09412a3609ca">alive, emotional depth, full of movement and hope（生き生きしている、深い感情、躍動感と希望）など、絵画から受ける感情を表現しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="41732313-761f-48dd-a6d1-604f6531f8ae" id="41732313-761f-48dd-a6d1-604f6531f8ae"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="d5623c8d-95bf-4247-a1c7-d814223c749c" id="d5623c8d-95bf-4247-a1c7-d814223c749c"><li><p name="9fab05ca-058d-47eb-a275-7d65e1a60ed9" id="9fab05ca-058d-47eb-a275-7d65e1a60ed9">vibrant（鮮やかな）</p></li><li><p name="3003e75a-6807-4f3e-8ab6-ddae8d4abc6a" id="3003e75a-6807-4f3e-8ab6-ddae8d4abc6a">bold（力強い）</p></li><li><p name="188f7344-002d-4d89-8499-4faaf49470a9" id="188f7344-002d-4d89-8499-4faaf49470a9">inspired（感動する）など、色彩や効果を表す語彙を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="c5b57926-335e-43a6-8b02-4869a799a3ac" id="c5b57926-335e-43a6-8b02-4869a799a3ac"><strong>結論</strong>：</p><ul name="f2aad553-a19a-4021-86ae-6c26c210b4d7" id="f2aad553-a19a-4021-86ae-6c26c210b4d7"><li><p name="eaef1348-e72b-4a83-83fe-6002dc061e81" id="eaef1348-e72b-4a83-83fe-6002dc061e81">beauty in darkness（暗闇の中の美）という概念で締めくくり、この作品への評価を述べています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="04299258-4837-4510-aa9d-3a0010c82505" id="04299258-4837-4510-aa9d-3a0010c82505">装置・技術 (Device/Technology)</h3><p name="82692eec-3e36-410f-964c-b6d859fde396" id="82692eec-3e36-410f-964c-b6d859fde396"><strong>質問例：</strong>“Describe a piece of (electrical or electronic) equipment in your home.”<br>「家にある電化製品のうち何か一つについて説明してください」<br><strong>模範回答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="0ebf8623-f9ad-4810-b4c6-6546c6136c72" id="0ebf8623-f9ad-4810-b4c6-6546c6136c72"><blockquote><p name="438785d1-06b9-49e3-8500-0b96999ca7b3" id="438785d1-06b9-49e3-8500-0b96999ca7b3">I’d like to describe my smartphone, which I use almost every day. <br><br>It’s a black device with a 6-inch touch screen. <br>I bought it about two years ago. <br>I use it to call, text, browse the internet, and even for navigation when I’m traveling. <br>Its battery lasts a whole day, so I don’t have to charge it frequently. <br><br>What’s important is that it helps me stay connected with family and friends through social media and messaging apps. <br>I think it’s indispensable because it also contains all my important information and reminders. <br><br>In conclusion, this smartphone is very useful and important to me in my daily life.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="00f0b0fb-2f00-4a95-a64c-cad4b2107a18" id="00f0b0fb-2f00-4a95-a64c-cad4b2107a18"><strong>解説：</strong></p><ul name="5c8c6a02-142c-45cb-a1c6-77fd7065d00d" id="5c8c6a02-142c-45cb-a1c6-77fd7065d00d"><li><p name="2f117191-9c09-4c9c-afe2-edbd338ab698" id="2f117191-9c09-4c9c-afe2-edbd338ab698"><strong>外観・使用歴：</strong></p><ul name="fa971d2c-fe52-44b4-8d90-eadf7db05c39" id="fa971d2c-fe52-44b4-8d90-eadf7db05c39"><li><p name="5001d6fd-ea58-4106-830f-36cc9d50c641" id="5001d6fd-ea58-4106-830f-36cc9d50c641">6-inch touch screen, bought it about two years ago（6インチのタッチスクリーン、2年前に購入）など機器の特徴を紹介しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="020007c8-e5ca-4108-a914-e1dd737fff48" id="020007c8-e5ca-4108-a914-e1dd737fff48"><strong>用途：</strong></p><ul name="ac656427-2969-4d7d-a15a-cbfa2589d060" id="ac656427-2969-4d7d-a15a-cbfa2589d060"><li><p name="9a21e470-7510-4cc1-bed1-46003aa23457" id="9a21e470-7510-4cc1-bed1-46003aa23457">call, text, browse the internet, navigation（通話、メール、ネット閲覧、ナビ）など具体的な使い方を列挙しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="3be47935-964f-42fa-941e-224a34ea63b8" id="3be47935-964f-42fa-941e-224a34ea63b8"><strong>重要性：</strong></p><ul name="b2e638c8-8f9c-4eb0-a84e-ca4dbad04775" id="b2e638c8-8f9c-4eb0-a84e-ca4dbad04775"><li><p name="c35a6b3c-a4f2-411e-a5c8-e9faa4fe193b" id="c35a6b3c-a4f2-411e-a5c8-e9faa4fe193b">stay connected, indispensable（つながりを保つ、不可欠）と、日常生活での必要性を強調しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="395d2fb7-d224-4c65-81cd-b28a04007b7b" id="395d2fb7-d224-4c65-81cd-b28a04007b7b"><strong>語彙：</strong></p><ul name="e29f1d71-ce8b-45b0-93bd-5bb03a5ea57d" id="e29f1d71-ce8b-45b0-93bd-5bb03a5ea57d"><li><p name="108557c8-734a-4a4e-ab7b-e15e67763503" id="108557c8-734a-4a4e-ab7b-e15e67763503">indispensable（絶対必要な）</p></li><li><p name="5be48b97-5347-4c85-b713-0957e77f3d0f" id="5be48b97-5347-4c85-b713-0957e77f3d0f">contains important information（重要な情報が入っている）など、機能面と感情面の表現を使用しています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><p name="73f2df20-7d57-4c6e-ba6e-8c2a76a679f8" id="73f2df20-7d57-4c6e-ba6e-8c2a76a679f8">各模範解答では、話の冒頭で<strong>導入フレーズ</strong>や時制を明確にし、5W1Hをカバーしています。<br>また、キーフレーズや具体例で描写を豊かにし、最後に感想や結論で締めくくっています。<br><br>練習する際は、上記のような構成と表現を参考にし、流暢かつ論理的にスピーチを行いましょう</p><hr><h2 name="53e34928-066f-4c79-af80-3ed387e78811" id="53e34928-066f-4c79-af80-3ed387e78811">Part3：抽象的・意見重視の問題への対応法</h2><figure name="7e503061-228d-49f8-85eb-1873614eb3c6" id="7e503061-228d-49f8-85eb-1873614eb3c6"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993438-nYB3WJ8XS6F7Koe2wUqp54Dv.png" alt="" width="620" height="408"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="5de85294-3e28-4d3d-9278-6ba42de0da2b" id="5de85294-3e28-4d3d-9278-6ba42de0da2b"><strong>概要</strong>：Part3ではPart2のテーマに関連した<strong>社会的・抽象的な問題</strong>について議論します。 <br>例えば、教育・環境・テクノロジーなど幅広い分野の問題提起や意見を問われます。<br><br>意見を述べるだけでなく、理由を説明し、比較や譲歩を交えて深く論じる能力が求められます。</p><hr><h3 name="bd9e8549-d1e3-4419-be48-61519c1605f5" id="bd9e8549-d1e3-4419-be48-61519c1605f5">✅ IELTSスピーキング頻出設問パターンと例文集</h3><ul name="107b8a57-3c17-4fb0-b613-dc7872379506" id="107b8a57-3c17-4fb0-b613-dc7872379506"><li><p name="0748dcb3-2f9a-4380-aa7d-3ccb25c6d369" id="0748dcb3-2f9a-4380-aa7d-3ccb25c6d369"><strong>意見表明 (Opinion)：</strong></p><ul name="264ba9c8-9498-4514-80d5-f1c602797c87" id="264ba9c8-9498-4514-80d5-f1c602797c87"><li><p name="cd815133-9970-4ec9-b2c3-8919a4c6b4bb" id="cd815133-9970-4ec9-b2c3-8919a4c6b4bb"><strong>自分の考え・感じ方を尋ねる質問</strong></p></li><li><p name="386e0c67-2853-4d00-904c-b949c9a99fc3" id="386e0c67-2853-4d00-904c-b949c9a99fc3">例文：What do you think about X?（Xについてどう思いますか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="52589a1b-cbbf-4d10-909d-632cb10ad00a" id="52589a1b-cbbf-4d10-909d-632cb10ad00a"><strong>同意・反対 (Agree/Disagree)：</strong></p><ul name="65cffab7-b7ba-4e4b-bd29-44b78f15c987" id="65cffab7-b7ba-4e4b-bd29-44b78f15c987"><li><p name="af380bac-b439-44eb-adad-e2de15863748" id="af380bac-b439-44eb-adad-e2de15863748"><strong>ある意見に賛成か反対かを尋ねる</strong></p></li><li><p name="3399c320-597f-46e7-bbd2-88aeef503f03" id="3399c320-597f-46e7-bbd2-88aeef503f03">例文：Do you agree that X is important?（Xは重要だと思いますか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="d3851c24-be2e-499f-9499-679a6f398952" id="d3851c24-be2e-499f-9499-679a6f398952"><strong>比較 / 対比 (Compare)：</strong></p><ul name="b4c1f0ca-19db-4ab9-b5d3-bb8f9f8fc629" id="b4c1f0ca-19db-4ab9-b5d3-bb8f9f8fc629"><li><p name="f5b9a6d0-9419-477e-b952-116c3ccee415" id="f5b9a6d0-9419-477e-b952-116c3ccee415"><strong>2つの物・状況の違いを比較する</strong></p></li><li><p name="cc2036e0-9980-4c9b-b3e4-4085bbd22fce" id="cc2036e0-9980-4c9b-b3e4-4085bbd22fce">例文：How is A different from B?（AはBとどう違いますか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="35f392a5-b29b-411d-9a60-2e4d7b41c812" id="35f392a5-b29b-411d-9a60-2e4d7b41c812"><strong>過去との比較 (Past)：</strong></p><ul name="05a4da6f-3b6d-41d0-8190-bea7dc0551e5" id="05a4da6f-3b6d-41d0-8190-bea7dc0551e5"><li><p name="c56afe1f-2ac8-4bcd-a5f3-228de698343e" id="c56afe1f-2ac8-4bcd-a5f3-228de698343e"><strong>過去と現在の変化を尋ねる</strong></p></li><li><p name="f573ff59-0340-49cc-aa64-a68bc34684eb" id="f573ff59-0340-49cc-aa64-a68bc34684eb">例文：How has X changed since the past?（昔と比べてXはどう変わりましたか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="e725609a-4764-439e-9113-5e65a7180d18" id="e725609a-4764-439e-9113-5e65a7180d18"><strong>二者択一 (Choice)：</strong></p><ul name="23a8dc59-797f-45ce-a187-166d3fc94b30" id="23a8dc59-797f-45ce-a187-166d3fc94b30"><li><p name="6f30387c-671d-4bea-8bbc-009996d746f1" id="6f30387c-671d-4bea-8bbc-009996d746f1"><strong>2つの選択肢のどちらが好ましいかを問う</strong></p></li><li><p name="dbbd0e8d-ecba-48b1-9dac-e241e871bbae" id="dbbd0e8d-ecba-48b1-9dac-e241e871bbae">例文：Which is better: A or B?（AとBのどちらがより良いですか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a965906a-6f59-46a5-b1f6-7b91f19216ef" id="a965906a-6f59-46a5-b1f6-7b91f19216ef"><strong>メリット・デメリット (Pros/Cons)：</strong></p><ul name="acc6a8fb-c5e1-4143-8c20-3f2ccd43b742" id="acc6a8fb-c5e1-4143-8c20-3f2ccd43b742"><li><p name="085e68c8-6243-4c6c-99eb-85ce3dc03281" id="085e68c8-6243-4c6c-99eb-85ce3dc03281"><strong>物事の長所と短所を考える</strong></p></li><li><p name="9bfc3db8-0704-4444-86fe-0937f7ad7e5f" id="9bfc3db8-0704-4444-86fe-0937f7ad7e5f">例文：What are the advantages and disadvantages of X?（Xの利点と欠点は？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="fd0281ff-8df0-4b89-bcb0-2b9725b10c1d" id="fd0281ff-8df0-4b89-bcb0-2b9725b10c1d"><strong>原因・結果 (Cause/Effect)：</strong></p><ul name="436f3900-ae8b-4e35-aa3a-6e28736de03d" id="436f3900-ae8b-4e35-aa3a-6e28736de03d"><li><p name="a222ac86-68fa-47a4-80f7-4e2f884b7c55" id="a222ac86-68fa-47a4-80f7-4e2f884b7c55"><strong>なぜそれが起きるのか／その影響は？</strong></p></li><li><p name="04380882-ac40-4114-9a55-544a0fcd54a5" id="04380882-ac40-4114-9a55-544a0fcd54a5">例文：Why do people do X? What effect does it have?（なぜ人々はXをするのか？その影響は？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="cde004e2-0714-43bb-b84f-f6831f884e43" id="cde004e2-0714-43bb-b84f-f6831f884e43"><strong>未来予測 (Future)：</strong></p><ul name="73eed0e4-d7f2-4168-8604-d6e207bbeff6" id="73eed0e4-d7f2-4168-8604-d6e207bbeff6"><li><p name="55bd723f-6ada-443b-bb0f-73d78c31a427" id="55bd723f-6ada-443b-bb0f-73d78c31a427"><strong>将来の予測や展望を語る</strong></p></li><li><p name="62f10468-79a0-4e59-86e2-76fcb9f97150" id="62f10468-79a0-4e59-86e2-76fcb9f97150">例文：What do you think will happen to X in the future?（将来Xはどうなると思いますか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="baa18809-67cf-478d-9dad-f4dbfb40a2df" id="baa18809-67cf-478d-9dad-f4dbfb40a2df"><strong>仮定 (Hypothetical)：</strong></p><ul name="8124a680-4fa4-4e8d-ba81-4183d6ca8b1f" id="8124a680-4fa4-4e8d-ba81-4183d6ca8b1f"><li><p name="9a374b33-1733-4b44-be2c-9b12ccd0fdb9" id="9a374b33-1733-4b44-be2c-9b12ccd0fdb9"><strong>もし～ならどうなるか、を想定する</strong></p></li><li><p name="ceb84c62-4a6d-4c2f-bc24-d923b2d803b4" id="ceb84c62-4a6d-4c2f-bc24-d923b2d803b4">例文：If X were to happen, what might the consequences be?（もしXが起きたら、その結果は？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="82e6854b-8ead-4ca9-81a4-261e8e9343ed" id="82e6854b-8ead-4ca9-81a4-261e8e9343ed"><strong>解決策・対策 (Solution)：</strong></p><ul name="11ff8c0d-4c7a-4b48-9785-84aad5168996" id="11ff8c0d-4c7a-4b48-9785-84aad5168996"><li><p name="af1ce150-b941-455a-9f28-9d18152e25f4" id="af1ce150-b941-455a-9f28-9d18152e25f4"><strong>問題への対応・解決法を提案する</strong></p></li><li><p name="be90d3b6-21f3-4858-8c53-a55d4009fb42" id="be90d3b6-21f3-4858-8c53-a55d4009fb42">例文：What should be done to solve X?（Xを解決するには何が必要ですか？）</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="8d248e28-1755-4ed4-9189-4335c8647061" id="8d248e28-1755-4ed4-9189-4335c8647061"><strong>例示・具体化 (Example)：</strong></p><ul name="3533aa4e-8c93-47f9-94c3-4713b50fc0c1" id="3533aa4e-8c93-47f9-94c3-4713b50fc0c1"><li><p name="5b2b8779-3dfb-4617-84b3-2a8425889c62" id="5b2b8779-3dfb-4617-84b3-2a8425889c62"><strong>具体例を求められる質問</strong></p></li><li><p name="f5cd72a9-9cd8-4b2d-b2e1-da107958e462" id="f5cd72a9-9cd8-4b2d-b2e1-da107958e462">例文：Can you give an example of X?（Xの例を挙げてください）</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><p name="388cc022-9b1c-4514-8d82-917a21985371" id="388cc022-9b1c-4514-8d82-917a21985371"><strong>回答のコツ：</strong></p><ul name="b8e10305-bbb7-4c2e-ac1a-4cc9fc83b662" id="b8e10305-bbb7-4c2e-ac1a-4cc9fc83b662"><li><p name="e799fa42-43ba-4142-8b27-1156b304bfa8" id="e799fa42-43ba-4142-8b27-1156b304bfa8"><strong>意見表明＋根拠：</strong></p><ul name="9dfc55c9-84a1-4a7a-bae0-ffaee1d03629" id="9dfc55c9-84a1-4a7a-bae0-ffaee1d03629"><li><p name="7165e8a9-5a12-49f6-9940-5ee38d9aff33" id="7165e8a9-5a12-49f6-9940-5ee38d9aff33">まず自分の立場や結論を“I think...”や“In my opinion...”で示し、その後で理由や例を展開します。</p><ul name="c5f154fe-5c14-4b1e-a38f-8361ed72885d" id="c5f154fe-5c14-4b1e-a38f-8361ed72885d"><li><p name="10861a59-577d-46fe-be7d-11013aecd958" id="10861a59-577d-46fe-be7d-11013aecd958">回答は論理的に箇条書きするイメージで、主張⇒理由①⇒理由②⇒まとめ、という構成を心がけます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="aae5ab52-25de-4a84-80f5-fc8dcec18267" id="aae5ab52-25de-4a84-80f5-fc8dcec18267"><strong>比較・対比表現：</strong></p><ul name="f7949c83-e73c-47df-b5fc-494302ee927b" id="f7949c83-e73c-47df-b5fc-494302ee927b"><li><p name="46451272-6432-4896-9a24-e3ed266fd96c" id="46451272-6432-4896-9a24-e3ed266fd96c">“On the one hand...”, “On the other hand...”, “in contrast”, “whereas” などで異なる意見や要素を並列に示します。</p><ul name="a7b3a53f-5a6e-4681-8a64-1fcae9b991b0" id="a7b3a53f-5a6e-4681-8a64-1fcae9b991b0"><li><p name="127a5cef-ab6b-4bb2-974e-5b7dc1322af7" id="127a5cef-ab6b-4bb2-974e-5b7dc1322af7">議論が複雑になる場合、「一方では～、他方では～」と比較することでバランスを取ります。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="e89d9059-c5d4-4ce0-979d-2497c10470f3" id="e89d9059-c5d4-4ce0-979d-2497c10470f3"><strong>譲歩表現：</strong></p><ul name="b90a037f-fa21-4a7d-b85a-0fc281e1490e" id="b90a037f-fa21-4a7d-b85a-0fc281e1490e"><li><p name="16ff9629-0691-4de2-b19d-34412f4025d0" id="16ff9629-0691-4de2-b19d-34412f4025d0">“Even though ~”, “Although ~”, “while ~”, “However” などを使い、一度相手側の見解を認めた上で自分の意見を述べます。</p><ul name="7028b22a-68b7-41b7-bd37-3d61876b3948" id="7028b22a-68b7-41b7-bd37-3d61876b3948"><li><p name="ce20e8eb-3438-4cad-ad39-bfaecb63f408" id="ce20e8eb-3438-4cad-ad39-bfaecb63f408">例えば “Although it’s true that ~, I believe...” の形です。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="1cc553e3-8a52-44d2-aa62-3aefb7d03157" id="1cc553e3-8a52-44d2-aa62-3aefb7d03157"><strong>因果・結論の表現：</strong></p><ul name="d9102daf-96ce-4e4f-afda-1c3ffe11eae8" id="d9102daf-96ce-4e4f-afda-1c3ffe11eae8"><li><p name="372ab61f-e378-43b0-a50c-ad517e1ebf4e" id="372ab61f-e378-43b0-a50c-ad517e1ebf4e">“because”, “therefore”, “as a result”, “consequently” などで、主張と理由の関係を明確に示します。</p><ul name="19641758-68a3-47a4-9962-5a0b5f512062" id="19641758-68a3-47a4-9962-5a0b5f512062"><li><p name="05381f07-ab89-4830-9670-941e0b3f1470" id="05381f07-ab89-4830-9670-941e0b3f1470">論理展開が分かりやすくなるよう、「～だから（because）」「その結果（as a result）」「したがって（therefore）」で結びつけます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="afadd37f-6387-4559-87b5-c05b090cffde" id="afadd37f-6387-4559-87b5-c05b090cffde"><strong>一般化と具体例：</strong></p><ul name="c182e2bb-21bb-41a0-ab85-f28540e068a4" id="c182e2bb-21bb-41a0-ab85-f28540e068a4"><li><p name="bba3bc41-cc04-49df-b971-8239f066bd6d" id="bba3bc41-cc04-49df-b971-8239f066bd6d">抽象的な問いには一般論と具体例の両面を交ぜて答えると説得力が増します。</p><ul name="b4c5729c-1475-41aa-878d-82860a8d5b8c" id="b4c5729c-1475-41aa-878d-82860a8d5b8c"><li><p name="4a64a709-d711-4e10-a2ce-8e215b30750c" id="4a64a709-d711-4e10-a2ce-8e215b30750c">“Generally speaking, ... For example, ...” と冒頭で大枠を述べ、続けて個別の例や自身の経験を挙げます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="1afba36d-653a-4b07-97f6-aad66d4839f2" id="1afba36d-653a-4b07-97f6-aad66d4839f2"><strong>語彙・表現：</strong></p><ul name="982d182e-04a1-406f-81e2-37e4b024e1fa" id="982d182e-04a1-406f-81e2-37e4b024e1fa"><li><p name="61605ee8-528e-4391-ba43-0514ff82862d" id="61605ee8-528e-4391-ba43-0514ff82862d">複数のアイデアを述べるために、“One advantage is...”, “Another drawback is...”, “Moreover”, “In addition”, “Therefore” などを使いましょう。</p><ul name="859160f8-5296-4e63-a627-f1d157d7de56" id="859160f8-5296-4e63-a627-f1d157d7de56"><li><p name="77540ce2-2d0b-4926-83ef-bc4a51bd1658" id="77540ce2-2d0b-4926-83ef-bc4a51bd1658">専門用語やテーマに関連する語彙が使えるとベターです。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="4f3d05b3-9e52-41b9-aca8-822c12cf5c3b" id="4f3d05b3-9e52-41b9-aca8-822c12cf5c3b"><strong>視点のバランス：</strong></p><ul name="7100b3e1-a6fa-4036-ae5c-7e23f0609435" id="7100b3e1-a6fa-4036-ae5c-7e23f0609435"><li><p name="afe096fb-e191-4d01-af95-1284d855fef7" id="afe096fb-e191-4d01-af95-1284d855fef7">自分の経験談や立場だけでなく、「多くの人々は～と考えている/研究によれば～とされる」など他者・一般論も交えると深みが出ます。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3 name="298be828-4ef5-47bb-814b-5896f6cb3445" id="298be828-4ef5-47bb-814b-5896f6cb3445">回答に使える「必勝フレーズ」チャンク</h3><figure name="8239aa78-54ae-4e4f-a404-880263adc1c2" id="8239aa78-54ae-4e4f-a404-880263adc1c2"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993491-KfPnZLBiVCAEv6340buyz9qc.png" alt="" width="620" height="382"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="eeb4d3ab-af90-4775-b386-638ecbf6abe2" id="eeb4d3ab-af90-4775-b386-638ecbf6abe2">Part3では論理的に長めの回答が求められるため、意見提示・理由付け・対比・例示といったフレーズを使って話を展開します。<br>以下にカテゴリ別の例を示します。</p><ul name="7e00eb11-ee8b-496f-9a99-8c2100cfb35e" id="7e00eb11-ee8b-496f-9a99-8c2100cfb35e"><li><p name="22a9003f-f033-428f-b245-2d38a5087a76" id="22a9003f-f033-428f-b245-2d38a5087a76"><strong>意見提示：</strong></p><ul name="95155455-5f1a-4246-9379-20fbb54a1e71" id="95155455-5f1a-4246-9379-20fbb54a1e71"><li><p name="fa0a6c3b-acc9-49b1-8ba4-3b39d422f32b" id="fa0a6c3b-acc9-49b1-8ba4-3b39d422f32b">「自分の意見」を述べる。</p><ul name="3073b294-b2e3-4a7c-a6ae-1abea15b3e73" id="3073b294-b2e3-4a7c-a6ae-1abea15b3e73"><li><p name="a25cd7e6-8c6a-4058-8ffb-ab79ca980801" id="a25cd7e6-8c6a-4058-8ffb-ab79ca980801">“In my opinion, …”</p></li><li><p name="2f035d64-133a-419e-8443-c2045ec442e6" id="2f035d64-133a-419e-8443-c2045ec442e6">“Personally, I think …”</p></li><li><p name="f2ecca93-5de2-4fe1-81cd-e465da6de09a" id="f2ecca93-5de2-4fe1-81cd-e465da6de09a">“I believe that …” など。<br>例: “<strong>Personally, I think</strong> technology has greatly improved our lives.”</p><ul name="363a9afa-da48-4022-b6a2-6a8fc1f7f156" id="363a9afa-da48-4022-b6a2-6a8fc1f7f156"><li><p name="c7dc6694-7b60-4cae-892f-99e51f1dd3a7" id="c7dc6694-7b60-4cae-892f-99e51f1dd3a7">※注意：毎回“I think…”だけで始めるのではなく、専門家も「繰り返し‘I think’で始めると印象が悪い」と指摘。</p></li><li><p name="1b84372f-575b-4b73-93e2-7a2bc433770f" id="1b84372f-575b-4b73-93e2-7a2bc433770f">上記のようにバリエーションを使います。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="379a8d70-38f7-4ac6-a463-40e58fb58b33" id="379a8d70-38f7-4ac6-a463-40e58fb58b33"><strong>理由付け・原因説明：</strong></p><ul name="69f0d431-ec38-4a7c-922c-9d84c43eab2a" id="69f0d431-ec38-4a7c-922c-9d84c43eab2a"><li><p name="aeb079c1-b0ce-459c-8395-520f034d436d" id="aeb079c1-b0ce-459c-8395-520f034d436d">理由や原因を示す。</p><ul name="dee9532c-e78d-4bd9-a84c-11519d6bc452" id="dee9532c-e78d-4bd9-a84c-11519d6bc452"><li><p name="2d579c71-8d51-48af-8aec-fd8e3624e565" id="2d579c71-8d51-48af-8aec-fd8e3624e565">“The main reason is that …”</p></li><li><p name="e6700cda-daaf-4443-b732-8f023727c148" id="e6700cda-daaf-4443-b732-8f023727c148">“This is because …”</p></li><li><p name="7a6c1c74-cc73-485b-a7d0-0f582a8ac635" id="7a6c1c74-cc73-485b-a7d0-0f582a8ac635">“It was caused by …”</p></li><li><p name="75404bf9-d44c-41e6-a83b-044def7300b8" id="75404bf9-d44c-41e6-a83b-044def7300b8">“I guess it’s because …”<br>例: “<strong>The main reason is that</strong> it creates many jobs.”</p><ul name="145a5885-4ffc-4451-a63a-019ab7408b53" id="145a5885-4ffc-4451-a63a-019ab7408b53"><li><p name="c7156db8-4ea4-4c6d-82da-2fa0cfbdef6d" id="c7156db8-4ea4-4c6d-82da-2fa0cfbdef6d">“because” や “due to” を使ってもOK。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="df9dfbba-8338-4f3b-91b4-00febc601179" id="df9dfbba-8338-4f3b-91b4-00febc601179"><strong>対比・譲歩</strong>：</p><ul name="147c15d2-973b-43de-8c9c-ec4ba073ac83" id="147c15d2-973b-43de-8c9c-ec4ba073ac83"><li><p name="087db182-674a-4da3-81bf-3e13ed9b876a" id="087db182-674a-4da3-81bf-3e13ed9b876a">反対意見や対立要素を示す。</p><ul name="f703c065-db33-471b-8b44-fbc63a58f8bd" id="f703c065-db33-471b-8b44-fbc63a58f8bd"><li><p name="1b00cd03-adfe-4c2e-9234-1ab31f1ac93f" id="1b00cd03-adfe-4c2e-9234-1ab31f1ac93f">“However, …”</p></li><li><p name="08094154-d8dd-4128-a01f-6c3a990720e1" id="08094154-d8dd-4128-a01f-6c3a990720e1">“On the other hand, …”</p></li><li><p name="d9389cad-5cac-4e8d-b803-07ae8e6612ce" id="d9389cad-5cac-4e8d-b803-07ae8e6612ce">“Although …, (yet) …”</p></li><li><p name="b5a59427-5e4e-40bb-8147-b0d3b0280cc9" id="b5a59427-5e4e-40bb-8147-b0d3b0280cc9">“While …, …” など。<br>例: “It has many benefits. <strong>However,</strong> there are some drawbacks.”</p><ul name="0f1666b7-ea9d-4422-8d62-e97d1770f0b7" id="0f1666b7-ea9d-4422-8d62-e97d1770f0b7"><li><p name="10269b64-2405-496e-a909-5cdc5c76a324" id="10269b64-2405-496e-a909-5cdc5c76a324">逆説の表現（でも／だが）で論点を切り替えます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="99b5ea1a-023a-4c15-9d43-8e6ca76c907d" id="99b5ea1a-023a-4c15-9d43-8e6ca76c907d"><strong>追加情報・列挙：</strong></p><ul name="fb055070-381e-4525-aad6-6a05f917a31b" id="fb055070-381e-4525-aad6-6a05f917a31b"><li><p name="f720d32f-4044-46d1-8363-09930cda083c" id="f720d32f-4044-46d1-8363-09930cda083c">話をつなげる。</p><ul name="e7fdaf65-1b8f-43ae-9668-c014e7dbce6a" id="e7fdaf65-1b8f-43ae-9668-c014e7dbce6a"><li><p name="1552044c-9654-49fe-8ca7-3ce6388b1d56" id="1552044c-9654-49fe-8ca7-3ce6388b1d56">“Also, …”</p></li><li><p name="ae94655f-5a38-4edc-892b-0d7c506345e7" id="ae94655f-5a38-4edc-892b-0d7c506345e7">“Furthermore, …”</p></li><li><p name="ac5332ab-36fc-4283-aa39-f5064bb9bb0c" id="ac5332ab-36fc-4283-aa39-f5064bb9bb0c">“Moreover, …”</p></li><li><p name="bce070ec-3bfb-41ec-8bb4-49052a563be8" id="bce070ec-3bfb-41ec-8bb4-49052a563be8">“In addition to that, …” など。<br>例: “The plan is cost-effective. <strong>Furthermore,</strong> it has environmental benefits.”</p><ul name="ffc09499-e26a-4a6e-9040-a09e04d2f47e" id="ffc09499-e26a-4a6e-9040-a09e04d2f47e"><li><p name="ec006fc3-f800-4a6f-997a-58ca64d82d89" id="ec006fc3-f800-4a6f-997a-58ca64d82d89">「さらに～」で情報を追加します。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="c1530c31-b154-4b32-a166-555d97b50dbf" id="c1530c31-b154-4b32-a166-555d97b50dbf"><strong>例示：</strong></p><ul name="cca3eefb-7373-46d3-a3f0-b172212064cb" id="cca3eefb-7373-46d3-a3f0-b172212064cb"><li><p name="bfeb1a92-9822-4894-a998-5ab9bb9574e7" id="bfeb1a92-9822-4894-a998-5ab9bb9574e7">具体例を挙げる。</p><ul name="0d161761-a1b0-4019-b550-5ed21348487a" id="0d161761-a1b0-4019-b550-5ed21348487a"><li><p name="d0240933-0122-418a-b920-a9e7c380afff" id="d0240933-0122-418a-b920-a9e7c380afff">“For example, …”</p></li><li><p name="03d92938-ba63-4394-b71c-5f541f438ae7" id="03d92938-ba63-4394-b71c-5f541f438ae7">“For instance, …”</p></li><li><p name="3351af15-9bb3-425e-bbaf-d04dc2f1d4c4" id="3351af15-9bb3-425e-bbaf-d04dc2f1d4c4">“Such as …”</p></li><li><p name="101065f0-3c1f-4451-bc09-d77d0a74ff40" id="101065f0-3c1f-4451-bc09-d77d0a74ff40">“A case in point is …”<br>例: “There are many renewable sources, <strong>for example,</strong> solar and wind power.”</p><ul name="f4cde9bd-b9c7-48e1-9b80-ac8b04479ef1" id="f4cde9bd-b9c7-48e1-9b80-ac8b04479ef1"><li><p name="e9d0c15c-9869-4b5a-bbf4-08d55294d635" id="e9d0c15c-9869-4b5a-bbf4-08d55294d635">事例や統計を示して説得力を高めます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="3eba3bfc-d170-47ab-8d82-321fe62768e3" id="3eba3bfc-d170-47ab-8d82-321fe62768e3"><strong>賛成・反対の強調：</strong></p><ul name="2d023c3c-8961-4543-bd5e-8fa809eae3f9" id="2d023c3c-8961-4543-bd5e-8fa809eae3f9"><li><p name="95ac95e6-39ed-4e27-b3b8-ba70aa01c007" id="95ac95e6-39ed-4e27-b3b8-ba70aa01c007">相手意見への同意・反対。</p><ul name="0f08f20b-6046-4a9b-8fba-60877049f42a" id="0f08f20b-6046-4a9b-8fba-60877049f42a"><li><p name="575e68d7-a4a9-44b4-8217-d84206a9cafe" id="575e68d7-a4a9-44b4-8217-d84206a9cafe">同意：</p><ul name="e7d7932e-bf51-47f2-aca2-8087184ac830" id="e7d7932e-bf51-47f2-aca2-8087184ac830"><li><p name="d005e9e5-495a-40e8-9616-fffbaef7603c" id="d005e9e5-495a-40e8-9616-fffbaef7603c">“I agree that …”</p></li><li><p name="098d1b99-72f2-4bde-b38a-ff46f8441c33" id="098d1b99-72f2-4bde-b38a-ff46f8441c33">“That’s true.”</p></li><li><p name="6985c765-a900-4a3e-a60e-8907ee106c27" id="6985c765-a900-4a3e-a60e-8907ee106c27">“I couldn’t agree more.”<br>例: “<strong>I agree that</strong> exercise is important for health.”</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="650908d4-ed09-4093-b8df-d24dea90f712" id="650908d4-ed09-4093-b8df-d24dea90f712">否定：</p><ul name="3b292a3c-e4db-40ab-97a3-491c07d653d8" id="3b292a3c-e4db-40ab-97a3-491c07d653d8"><li><p name="eaadf965-8ea1-435d-9f07-93d7b26255b0" id="eaadf965-8ea1-435d-9f07-93d7b26255b0">“I’m afraid I disagree.”</p></li><li><p name="2cbbcb7b-571c-468f-892a-8d662eedd89d" id="2cbbcb7b-571c-468f-892a-8d662eedd89d">“I don’t think so.”</p></li><li><p name="82e47072-a454-4a0f-a32b-f37fb7eb9538" id="82e47072-a454-4a0f-a32b-f37fb7eb9538">“I beg to differ.”<br>例: “<strong>I disagree.</strong> I believe education is important for everyone.”</p><ul name="0f7598d3-4a13-4b5f-bf75-c8ebe1f2b2d4" id="0f7598d3-4a13-4b5f-bf75-c8ebe1f2b2d4"><li><p name="ed67bb2d-8f6c-422d-8650-cbe118ffee0b" id="ed67bb2d-8f6c-422d-8650-cbe118ffee0b">反対意見を述べる際に使います。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="04d5cb0e-4d7d-46ac-9350-0a31e992563b" id="04d5cb0e-4d7d-46ac-9350-0a31e992563b"><strong>回答開始・結論：</strong></p><ul name="56023248-64a8-45a3-ab7b-13b28b14c4a6" id="56023248-64a8-45a3-ab7b-13b28b14c4a6"><li><p name="887a35de-1163-4de3-88b1-24a99910809b" id="887a35de-1163-4de3-88b1-24a99910809b">質問を受け止めたり要点をまとめる表現。</p><ul name="c6147605-f314-4c04-932e-90fb28d07c32" id="c6147605-f314-4c04-932e-90fb28d07c32"><li><p name="c7e64847-e704-415a-b9e3-d82d006fd94e" id="c7e64847-e704-415a-b9e3-d82d006fd94e">“That’s an interesting question…”</p></li><li><p name="de0c64d5-4b61-405b-9605-2504a7144803" id="de0c64d5-4b61-405b-9605-2504a7144803">“I haven’t thought about it that way, but …”<br>例: “That’s an interesting question. I think …”</p><ul name="e6d16e48-bc89-4c04-a789-bb03fbabe773" id="e6d16e48-bc89-4c04-a789-bb03fbabe773"><li><p name="32751721-9ebf-4110-b812-ced91bf8cd23" id="32751721-9ebf-4110-b812-ced91bf8cd23">述べ始めや結論で使い、話を滑らかにつなぎます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul><p name="b03075fa-df89-4d5b-99a3-0188a5e5829e" id="b03075fa-df89-4d5b-99a3-0188a5e5829e"><strong>ポイント：</strong>フレーズは自然な範囲で使うことが重要です。 <br>例えば「because」や「so」などは日常会話でも使いやすいため、くどくならない程度に繰り返しても構いません。 <br>また、スピーキングでは専門家も「繰り返し単語を使っても減点されない」と述べています。</p><hr><p name="309b5948-c6c1-479d-9553-40b7e815d31c" id="309b5948-c6c1-479d-9553-40b7e815d31c"><strong>例1：</strong> “What are the advantages and disadvantages of working from home?”<br><strong>模範解答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="7c808d4c-cdb8-4aca-98d4-4ebe19233967" id="7c808d4c-cdb8-4aca-98d4-4ebe19233967"><blockquote><p name="6b8c6a42-186c-4a8c-b6cc-e6d11f8eecc8" id="6b8c6a42-186c-4a8c-b6cc-e6d11f8eecc8">In my opinion, working from home <strong>offers</strong> both benefits and challenges. <br>On the one hand, it provides great flexibility and saves commuting time. <br>For example, employees can spend those extra hours with family or on personal projects, which can improve work-life balance. <br><br>On the other hand, remote work may lead to feelings of isolation and blurred boundaries between work and private life. <br>Although video calls and messaging tools help us stay connected, nothing fully replaces face-to-face interaction with colleagues. <br><br>Another disadvantage is that some people might end up working longer hours because their home becomes their office. <br><br>Therefore, while remote work provides convenience, it’s important to set strict schedules and take breaks to maintain productivity and well-being.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><ul name="263d0cdc-3101-4a36-a818-0994b6fb4dc0" id="263d0cdc-3101-4a36-a818-0994b6fb4dc0"><li><p name="d3d4035f-cf30-4dce-b978-122a552c93cc" id="d3d4035f-cf30-4dce-b978-122a552c93cc"><strong>構成</strong>：</p><ul name="6bbc72a3-b4f6-4d9b-86ce-2f2ce7d37976" id="6bbc72a3-b4f6-4d9b-86ce-2f2ce7d37976"><li><p name="77c0aefc-f070-49de-a0c6-33edf39f0dd3" id="77c0aefc-f070-49de-a0c6-33edf39f0dd3">冒頭で自分の意見（利点と欠点がある）を示し、On the one hand... On the other hand... と対比を入れて説明、最後にまとめて結論づけています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="2ee79284-f165-454c-9456-536c56be9c35" id="2ee79284-f165-454c-9456-536c56be9c35"><strong>語彙・表現</strong>：</p><ul name="f2769bf0-4959-46b4-83a4-9c8f85ebbf6f" id="f2769bf0-4959-46b4-83a4-9c8f85ebbf6f"><li><p name="fbd576f4-605c-4fb7-9c8f-00e0c521899f" id="fbd576f4-605c-4fb7-9c8f-00e0c521899f">offers</p></li><li><p name="b9e88a21-7f8f-4d2c-842f-ab91317f12e4" id="b9e88a21-7f8f-4d2c-842f-ab91317f12e4">benefits</p></li><li><p name="4bd188ea-ff15-4821-a894-5fe08820caad" id="4bd188ea-ff15-4821-a894-5fe08820caad">challenges</p></li><li><p name="a8aafea3-1402-434a-a9df-8c75c2f70f95" id="a8aafea3-1402-434a-a9df-8c75c2f70f95">flexibility</p></li><li><p name="7fb38fa0-f016-4014-b8a6-4683b504698d" id="7fb38fa0-f016-4014-b8a6-4683b504698d">commuting</p></li><li><p name="69aa6252-4c7b-48ae-a8a2-fbe1113ca92f" id="69aa6252-4c7b-48ae-a8a2-fbe1113ca92f">improve</p></li><li><p name="4978ea04-d492-45d1-940f-2fdf462d2249" id="4978ea04-d492-45d1-940f-2fdf462d2249">isolation</p></li><li><p name="67b5b628-775d-4ebb-a6bf-6978a6079bcb" id="67b5b628-775d-4ebb-a6bf-6978a6079bcb">blurs (boundaries)</p></li><li><p name="4e37c114-2eb9-46ee-969b-0488c499bed9"
