id="4e37c114-2eb9-46ee-969b-0488c499bed9">replaces</p></li><li><p name="4398f616-9072-47c2-9e12-487f428e29a0" id="4398f616-9072-47c2-9e12-487f428e29a0">disadvantage</p></li><li><p name="d131bd40-f523-48e8-a850-95c97aad7ed9" id="d131bd40-f523-48e8-a850-95c97aad7ed9">maintain productivity など。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="05a040be-8e49-47f6-a17f-21e5873f3a73" id="05a040be-8e49-47f6-a17f-21e5873f3a73"><strong>接続詞・チャンク</strong>：</p><ul name="b93fa97c-6af5-4119-8b6a-856412c239c3" id="b93fa97c-6af5-4119-8b6a-856412c239c3"><li><p name="f97dbcc1-3b2d-423c-842e-9028af82aa43" id="f97dbcc1-3b2d-423c-842e-9028af82aa43">On the one hand</p></li><li><p name="55d1fbe0-7c98-425d-8e3c-2c021390b616" id="55d1fbe0-7c98-425d-8e3c-2c021390b616">On the other hand</p></li><li><p name="f2350bca-97c7-4061-92fc-4230f7f6b096" id="f2350bca-97c7-4061-92fc-4230f7f6b096">For example</p></li><li><p name="a552035c-8f15-4ef3-b019-14f0e00894a1" id="a552035c-8f15-4ef3-b019-14f0e00894a1">Although</p></li><li><p name="e667043f-3b8d-499b-98c3-35a5b641f462" id="e667043f-3b8d-499b-98c3-35a5b641f462">Another disadvantage</p></li><li><p name="ad108a54-3a53-4fc1-909d-8064b2dc8cea" id="ad108a54-3a53-4fc1-909d-8064b2dc8cea">Therefore などを使用し、意見間の流れを明示しています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a459c36a-7718-4234-babc-45cdaa34f7d1" id="a459c36a-7718-4234-babc-45cdaa34f7d1"><strong>ヘッジ</strong>：</p><ul name="108f5e25-5006-49ae-b78d-ac86c4c2154f" id="108f5e25-5006-49ae-b78d-ac86c4c2154f"><li><p name="7d52c1d1-de75-47b8-baa2-7fb0fddd3c6a" id="7d52c1d1-de75-47b8-baa2-7fb0fddd3c6a">I believe, might, may などで断定を和らげています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="0e80f911-568a-4cf4-84b8-304b03efb075" id="0e80f911-568a-4cf4-84b8-304b03efb075"><strong>5W1H</strong>：</p><ul name="da7d993a-2b7a-4a46-8065-8bae9363ba93" id="da7d993a-2b7a-4a46-8065-8bae9363ba93"><li><p name="8bbc6879-564e-4de9-bd34-b261dac4ffcf" id="8bbc6879-564e-4de9-bd34-b261dac4ffcf">whenやwhoは明示していませんが、状況設定としてリモートワークの一般例を挙げ、具体例（家族との時間、コミュニケーション手段）を加えています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><hr><p name="fc8b6396-521d-463e-8edd-4c2f319d2c6f" id="fc8b6396-521d-463e-8edd-4c2f319d2c6f"><strong>例2：</strong> “Do you think teenagers today face more pressure than in the past? Why?”<br><strong>模範解答（英語）:</strong></p><figure name="7d449dd9-8af4-4a2e-8159-c6db5404445b" id="7d449dd9-8af4-4a2e-8159-c6db5404445b"><blockquote><p name="3d72a739-835b-4f28-b85a-3a13d9c10ce6" id="3d72a739-835b-4f28-b85a-3a13d9c10ce6"><strong>Nowadays</strong>, I think teenagers do face more pressure compared to the past. <br><br>Firstly, social media is a big factor. <br>On the one hand, it provides them with information and a way to stay connected. <br>On the other hand, it exposes them to constant comparison. <br>For example, many teens might feel insecure when they see peers posting about their achievements or lifestyle. <br><br>Moreover, academic competition and parental expectations have also increased. <br>Even though competition can motivate some students to work harder, it can cause stress and anxiety for others. <br><br>Therefore, while modern technology brings opportunities, it’s important for young people to learn time management and coping strategies to handle pressure.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><ul name="07fd1d1a-86bc-4801-a6a5-88c01b73478d" id="07fd1d1a-86bc-4801-a6a5-88c01b73478d"><li><p name="def9c589-f734-4cf7-849f-097b70c5d7ed" id="def9c589-f734-4cf7-849f-097b70c5d7ed"><strong>構成</strong>：</p><ul name="4390f655-c2be-4491-adb7-0d16c7062a72" id="4390f655-c2be-4491-adb7-0d16c7062a72"><li><p name="8df314ed-eff2-4610-8092-bbdf451dc01e" id="8df314ed-eff2-4610-8092-bbdf451dc01e">冒頭で現在の状況を述べ、Firstly から要因を順に説明、最後にまとめています。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="8e21651b-c9d8-4c19-9e9d-2dbd5f4cb423" id="8e21651b-c9d8-4c19-9e9d-2dbd5f4cb423"><strong>語彙・表現</strong>：</p><ul name="272cd515-53e2-490d-b615-19caa2298dec" id="272cd515-53e2-490d-b615-19caa2298dec"><li><p name="188f70e1-f48d-47e0-8125-50c2aef822b0" id="188f70e1-f48d-47e0-8125-50c2aef822b0">nowadays</p></li><li><p name="3e604d20-0744-4e75-89bb-d13f3f8ba8e6" id="3e604d20-0744-4e75-89bb-d13f3f8ba8e6">pressure</p></li><li><p name="d45d0f78-111d-41c1-afee-aad39b80d705" id="d45d0f78-111d-41c1-afee-aad39b80d705">social media</p></li><li><p name="eb1c695e-a13d-4d4b-97c9-a23b9866eadd" id="eb1c695e-a13d-4d4b-97c9-a23b9866eadd">provide information</p></li><li><p name="413abc98-4104-4833-8070-d3ca37203540" id="413abc98-4104-4833-8070-d3ca37203540">connected</p></li><li><p name="5c84f7ac-78d5-4848-8693-fe8b676492b3" id="5c84f7ac-78d5-4848-8693-fe8b676492b3">expose</p></li><li><p name="118d29c3-b46c-4927-a451-d387991614a1" id="118d29c3-b46c-4927-a451-d387991614a1">constant comparison</p></li><li><p name="d3f0805a-fb78-4fc1-a32c-0e988092172c" id="d3f0805a-fb78-4fc1-a32c-0e988092172c">academic competition</p></li><li><p name="2ae5a2b7-add4-493d-90aa-bb4f71ac3abf" id="2ae5a2b7-add4-493d-90aa-bb4f71ac3abf">expectations</p></li><li><p name="009ff209-85f5-4c39-9281-2d00799ff368" id="009ff209-85f5-4c39-9281-2d00799ff368">stress</p></li><li><p name="c2366426-5f8b-4211-81fc-691034911472" id="c2366426-5f8b-4211-81fc-691034911472">time management など。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="eb0fe131-ce20-4c08-ae7a-fe2098aa34f5" id="eb0fe131-ce20-4c08-ae7a-fe2098aa34f5"><strong>接続詞・チャンク</strong>：</p><ul name="b98ae786-1ab5-4fbe-9452-0425608a7f4c" id="b98ae786-1ab5-4fbe-9452-0425608a7f4c"><li><p name="4c153062-8fb7-47ed-946f-d9df13d81463" id="4c153062-8fb7-47ed-946f-d9df13d81463">On the one hand</p></li><li><p name="5299b550-6377-494c-af2c-c4899c276d78" id="5299b550-6377-494c-af2c-c4899c276d78">On the other hand</p></li><li><p name="afff0d09-eff8-4c24-a348-bb6b1c60520c" id="afff0d09-eff8-4c24-a348-bb6b1c60520c">For example</p></li><li><p name="e543be9c-c205-48cf-b07c-863a2dcf5272" id="e543be9c-c205-48cf-b07c-863a2dcf5272">Moreover</p></li><li><p name="bd28370f-f9bc-4d99-abc7-68e90f47e815" id="bd28370f-f9bc-4d99-abc7-68e90f47e815">Even though</p></li><li><p name="21768030-1d11-4ac1-9557-b596a62c8234" id="21768030-1d11-4ac1-9557-b596a62c8234">Therefore など、多様な繋ぎ語を使用。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="d2b0635e-f51a-4e0f-a6d9-b85d468254e7" id="d2b0635e-f51a-4e0f-a6d9-b85d468254e7"><strong>5W1H</strong>：</p><ul name="3245cf1b-297b-4da4-a2f2-f30a0616c8aa" id="3245cf1b-297b-4da4-a2f2-f30a0616c8aa"><li><p name="e1b1b950-6c2e-401b-bd24-f622e79a5622" id="e1b1b950-6c2e-401b-bd24-f622e79a5622">一般論として語りつつ「many teens」など対象を明示し、具体例（SNS上の投稿、勉強競争）を挙げています。</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="18074bd4-58c4-4fbe-a064-011fc37ede25" id="18074bd4-58c4-4fbe-a064-011fc37ede25"><blockquote><p name="303bbc4e-ede0-4643-971a-9db4bf276746" id="303bbc4e-ede0-4643-971a-9db4bf276746">参考：<br>・専門家によれば、Part3の代表的な質問タイプとして「意見」「仮定」「比較・対比」「変化」「未来」「利点」などが挙げられています。<br>・また、広告の話題では「Which are more effective: adverts on TV or on social media?」（TV広告とネット広告、どちらが効果的か）、服装の話題では「What are the advantages and disadvantages of having uniforms at work?」（仕事で制服を着るメリットとデメリットは？）のような質問も典型例です。</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="3fdcff7e-b19e-4039-8ed7-a70c1c2816b6" id="3fdcff7e-b19e-4039-8ed7-a70c1c2816b6">トピック別代表質問例・対策</h3><p name="e8cb6a60-7fe0-449d-ab7a-347c286d3b61" id="e8cb6a60-7fe0-449d-ab7a-347c286d3b61">以下に主要トピックごとの代表的なPart3質問例（英語）を挙げ、回答の切り口や語彙例、（可能な場合は）模範回答を示します。</p><h3 name="3a758b2f-003b-42ff-a9e0-0a75b347a2d1" id="3a758b2f-003b-42ff-a9e0-0a75b347a2d1">テクノロジー (Technology)</h3><ul name="5c26d968-a02d-489b-900e-8a00220db193" id="5c26d968-a02d-489b-900e-8a00220db193"><li><p name="7cfd46b5-4ab4-40ea-9d99-686a3aa4f851" id="7cfd46b5-4ab4-40ea-9d99-686a3aa4f851"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="0512570c-ae97-4ffa-933c-092b09f970f6" id="0512570c-ae97-4ffa-933c-092b09f970f6"><li><p name="0b72b9c5-fb77-4883-a75c-3825c73b8595" id="0b72b9c5-fb77-4883-a75c-3825c73b8595">What modern technological devices are most common in your country?</p></li><li><p name="6ee4144f-427f-41d8-8925-a6dbd0474354" id="6ee4144f-427f-41d8-8925-a6dbd0474354">Do you think people rely too much on technology?</p></li><li><p name="babc1871-7781-4e29-b9a3-c769e99d8bd1" id="babc1871-7781-4e29-b9a3-c769e99d8bd1">Why do you think people spend so much money buying the latest devices?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="6112da29-2901-4a88-9b16-092219dc55a4" id="6112da29-2901-4a88-9b16-092219dc55a4"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="6bf58806-8347-4f62-8d44-c57fd468e421" id="6bf58806-8347-4f62-8d44-c57fd468e421"><li><p name="d0dfeea7-297d-4662-b5d2-37f6591e26f7" id="d0dfeea7-297d-4662-b5d2-37f6591e26f7"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="aa80a4b7-f798-4b80-a9f7-67932d54000c" id="aa80a4b7-f798-4b80-a9f7-67932d54000c"><li><p name="3e8816f7-af62-48a9-8f6f-9dee3f76d7f3" id="3e8816f7-af62-48a9-8f6f-9dee3f76d7f3">新技術の利点（効率性、利便性）と欠点（依存、失業増加）を対比。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="75338546-160c-4d3c-ba21-e7a8c3a99bd3" id="75338546-160c-4d3c-ba21-e7a8c3a99bd3"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="a7425984-cbce-4f15-9b54-e42476d60ce1" id="a7425984-cbce-4f15-9b54-e42476d60ce1"><li><p name="25ba7863-0ca1-424c-9cf7-1a4cbec6057a" id="25ba7863-0ca1-424c-9cf7-1a4cbec6057a">gadget</p></li><li><p name="e7d121cb-25f9-4d86-af89-4a768238d6dc" id="e7d121cb-25f9-4d86-af89-4a768238d6dc">innovation</p></li><li><p name="809949f7-0a89-4503-8334-b00e3b622500" id="809949f7-0a89-4503-8334-b00e3b622500">dependence</p></li><li><p name="ba4f800c-5adf-4fbc-b61b-a499f0d4b2ee" id="ba4f800c-5adf-4fbc-b61b-a499f0d4b2ee">connectivity</p></li><li><p name="d589d41d-f10c-4cc7-a09f-6a2ee0aa91e5" id="d589d41d-f10c-4cc7-a09f-6a2ee0aa91e5">obsolete など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="cf5ffba1-28a6-4cb0-b4e1-c6cad619c897" id="cf5ffba1-28a6-4cb0-b4e1-c6cad619c897"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="4dc87083-e2d3-4c99-b6f1-8eee08c1d6d9" id="4dc87083-e2d3-4c99-b6f1-8eee08c1d6d9"><li><p name="bdd201dc-b86c-4cde-b6ca-78278ff41ff7" id="bdd201dc-b86c-4cde-b6ca-78278ff41ff7">Q： Do you think people rely too much on technology?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="ec1cbb7c-5040-42ec-a578-40d58aa437d2" id="ec1cbb7c-5040-42ec-a578-40d58aa437d2"><blockquote><p name="08827530-b665-43e4-a59b-a371c68c58c3" id="08827530-b665-43e4-a59b-a371c68c58c3">A：<br>Yes, to some extent. <br>Technology has made our lives easier in many ways, but <strong>I worry</strong> that people now spend too much time on devices instead of face-to-face interaction. <br><strong>For example</strong>, many adults and children are addicted to smartphones. <br><strong>However,</strong> it’s also true that modern devices have enabled remote work and global communication, which wouldn’t be possible otherwise. <br><br><strong>Personally,</strong> I try to balance my screen time by taking regular breaks.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="89b2200f-677e-4aed-96fb-1b3de7f5e45a" id="89b2200f-677e-4aed-96fb-1b3de7f5e45a">教育 (Education)</h3><ul name="f63f0231-b7e4-4f4a-9249-59d24596e387" id="f63f0231-b7e4-4f4a-9249-59d24596e387"><li><p name="8b59fda8-7a5a-4937-9dfe-9b5680f7eedd" id="8b59fda8-7a5a-4937-9dfe-9b5680f7eedd"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="d8583bfc-130e-42a7-bfa7-4a356735fbc1" id="d8583bfc-130e-42a7-bfa7-4a356735fbc1"><li><p name="54400ab9-4a9a-47d2-a0d0-dea7817f0ea5" id="54400ab9-4a9a-47d2-a0d0-dea7817f0ea5">Do you think computers will one day replace teachers in the classroom?</p></li><li><p name="c43f229e-0799-4f27-aa0a-9d59293d2e4b" id="c43f229e-0799-4f27-aa0a-9d59293d2e4b">How has teaching changed in your country in the last few decades?</p></li><li><p name="59728d63-21dc-4a31-a218-beca85f06c93" id="59728d63-21dc-4a31-a218-beca85f06c93">Is it easier to learn as a child or as an adult?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="feaac8c4-0021-4ab0-8381-0db9d06dabde" id="feaac8c4-0021-4ab0-8381-0db9d06dabde"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="a813adfc-3313-45f4-a49e-be76b0576204" id="a813adfc-3313-45f4-a49e-be76b0576204"><li><p name="a572f915-455c-42fe-872f-956f32cb52f4" id="a572f915-455c-42fe-872f-956f32cb52f4"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="5be354d2-24f1-4fb8-ac26-7a6e7148b27b" id="5be354d2-24f1-4fb8-ac26-7a6e7148b27b"><li><p name="6328c3cf-e032-4e39-b68a-7d5df3269772" id="6328c3cf-e032-4e39-b68a-7d5df3269772"><strong>&nbsp;</strong>テクノロジー教育 vs. 人間教師、学習方法の変化（オンライン教育・アクティブラーニング）。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="cf392c01-5ab4-489c-bf9e-19e0fc5fc202" id="cf392c01-5ab4-489c-bf9e-19e0fc5fc202"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="cb5e2fc7-999c-4bf8-a6cb-3d87de26b8c9" id="cb5e2fc7-999c-4bf8-a6cb-3d87de26b8c9"><li><p name="83b84d7e-4752-4419-80c0-2f7fbd39c072" id="83b84d7e-4752-4419-80c0-2f7fbd39c072">curriculum</p></li><li><p name="a11ae7ee-f59c-4e32-b9a5-e5825fc55534" id="a11ae7ee-f59c-4e32-b9a5-e5825fc55534">e-learning</p></li><li><p name="8e78f12a-3c20-4c25-ae7e-de927e506242" id="8e78f12a-3c20-4c25-ae7e-de927e506242">interactive</p></li><li><p name="72b4c573-21e7-4532-a911-039438cb9e67" id="72b4c573-21e7-4532-a911-039438cb9e67">lifelong learning</p></li><li><p name="98477ba5-d452-44e3-b359-2f9b7592b8d2" id="98477ba5-d452-44e3-b359-2f9b7592b8d2">student-centered など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="6db07cd7-089a-49a8-873a-1b16833d8832" id="6db07cd7-089a-49a8-873a-1b16833d8832"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="1056a11b-9733-4688-99ca-221b0e03c853" id="1056a11b-9733-4688-99ca-221b0e03c853"><li><p name="2de4005f-34d4-4290-96d6-4d23b03ddd70" id="2de4005f-34d4-4290-96d6-4d23b03ddd70">Q：Do you think computers will one day replace teachers?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="48ce6fd0-a981-43ee-a865-ed17a78e48eb" id="48ce6fd0-a981-43ee-a865-ed17a78e48eb"><blockquote><p name="e0207cde-2f87-4d6c-b8b3-68874227b1e1" id="e0207cde-2f87-4d6c-b8b3-68874227b1e1">A：<br>I <strong>doubt</strong> that computers can fully replace human teachers. <br><strong>In my opinion,</strong> technology is a great tool for education, but <strong>the personal touch</strong> of a teacher is irreplaceable. <br><strong>For example,</strong> a teacher can understand a student’s emotional needs and tailor explanations accordingly. <br><strong>However,</strong> computers can supplement learning by providing interactive exercises and instant feedback. <br>So I think a balance of both is ideal.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="d4a34cc9-9f29-46d3-95ec-8675a8b2f4ef" id="d4a34cc9-9f29-46d3-95ec-8675a8b2f4ef">環境 (Environment)</h3><ul name="0379a34b-d744-4eec-b613-508f12d4cbe3" id="0379a34b-d744-4eec-b613-508f12d4cbe3"><li><p name="f8abc4c5-37ee-4f4d-b117-82ca5e62a020" id="f8abc4c5-37ee-4f4d-b117-82ca5e62a020"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="9ec748f7-2724-4012-9973-546f38ce8b98" id="9ec748f7-2724-4012-9973-546f38ce8b98"><li><p name="3d3f2a19-9ae8-4beb-a1dd-5ca0a98278e6" id="3d3f2a19-9ae8-4beb-a1dd-5ca0a98278e6">What are the biggest environmental problems in your country?</p></li><li><p name="c65dd0f8-7aa7-47b4-8d54-a2a7e49a2fd5" id="c65dd0f8-7aa7-47b4-8d54-a2a7e49a2fd5">What should individuals be doing to protect the natural environment?</p></li><li><p name="65c38bf2-55f5-4933-a6ae-756b4e4be297" id="65c38bf2-55f5-4933-a6ae-756b4e4be297">Do you think more money should be spent on protecting wild animals?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="4f761dc8-c5e7-4a85-91e0-d131d48cd3e3" id="4f761dc8-c5e7-4a85-91e0-d131d48cd3e3"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="88d6e9ad-e3e4-422c-b0fe-08972ba5d692" id="88d6e9ad-e3e4-422c-b0fe-08972ba5d692"><li><p name="4a29ff24-9e9d-4d2f-b986-56ca9e467e5d" id="4a29ff24-9e9d-4d2f-b986-56ca9e467e5d"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="49b596b3-8f27-4b08-92f5-14f6b724c4a1" id="49b596b3-8f27-4b08-92f5-14f6b724c4a1"><li><p name="5b4d95c9-7cb1-42c6-91f2-d4a8390dbe22" id="5b4d95c9-7cb1-42c6-91f2-d4a8390dbe22">汚染・気候変動問題について個人と政府の役割、再生可能エネルギーやリサイクルの重要性を説明。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a6b08bf5-9ad2-4878-952b-4493a33c000b" id="a6b08bf5-9ad2-4878-952b-4493a33c000b"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="009b17ee-3f9a-4d87-8144-a4acbf09ba4e" id="009b17ee-3f9a-4d87-8144-a4acbf09ba4e"><li><p name="eba44eab-de7e-45a4-812e-2613b23124d5" id="eba44eab-de7e-45a4-812e-2613b23124d5">pollution</p></li><li><p name="c139b4e5-60d2-4e40-888d-17d0b36511f6" id="c139b4e5-60d2-4e40-888d-17d0b36511f6">renewable energy</p></li><li><p name="74f86fcc-0228-4dcf-8018-2b65034516f4" id="74f86fcc-0228-4dcf-8018-2b65034516f4">sustainability</p></li><li><p name="8cd5255d-d2db-44db-b7ca-c280a7006611" id="8cd5255d-d2db-44db-b7ca-c280a7006611">conservation</p></li><li><p name="3feb8c22-bf87-4ebb-baa8-2babc205ecc8" id="3feb8c22-bf87-4ebb-baa8-2babc205ecc8">emission など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="8536ad15-4533-4162-bab9-367486e57e11" id="8536ad15-4533-4162-bab9-367486e57e11"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="4311ec06-0a72-449e-b8a2-1408c95beff7" id="4311ec06-0a72-449e-b8a2-1408c95beff7"><li><p name="3bccb074-a303-48a3-8b85-6bb12436dd8d" id="3bccb074-a303-48a3-8b85-6bb12436dd8d">Q：What should individuals be doing to protect the environment?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="b007eeb0-af94-43a9-8b54-23169409c532" id="b007eeb0-af94-43a9-8b54-23169409c532"><blockquote><p name="fb31f45a-e35e-4230-b966-1e83d01084b0" id="fb31f45a-e35e-4230-b966-1e83d01084b0">A：<br>Individuals have <strong>several roles</strong>. <br><strong>First,</strong> they can reduce waste by recycling and using reusable bags. <br><strong>For example,</strong> many people choose cloth bags over plastic to cut down on landfill waste. <br><strong>In addition,</strong> using public transport or bikes instead of cars can lower carbon emissions. <br><strong>However,</strong> real change also requires government support, like providing recycling programs and green energy incentives. <br>So it’s a mix of personal action and policy.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="ad65e332-0a37-4b56-8031-5e743bb5a421" id="ad65e332-0a37-4b56-8031-5e743bb5a421">健康 (Health)</h3><ul name="7d666b56-0ace-4031-8f34-e9ffe6d7e807" id="7d666b56-0ace-4031-8f34-e9ffe6d7e807"><li><p name="fc1104f6-dcfc-46b8-8c57-0ecf92ef01d8" id="fc1104f6-dcfc-46b8-8c57-0ecf92ef01d8"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="302a8053-5ce5-4acf-9d95-b8bb7e4ce624" id="302a8053-5ce5-4acf-9d95-b8bb7e4ce624"><li><p name="d6c6d29d-7257-4643-8425-046d627bad0b" id="d6c6d29d-7257-4643-8425-046d627bad0b">How can people improve their health?</p></li><li><p name="14dffe31-88fe-4e6a-ba6f-c0cd5f015c36" id="14dffe31-88fe-4e6a-ba6f-c0cd5f015c36">Do elderly people do much exercise in your country?</p></li><li><p name="4f39831d-7495-4208-ab68-b66ea9697403" id="4f39831d-7495-4208-ab68-b66ea9697403">Do you think health care should be free?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="5c17eb9e-9d8e-4499-9a96-e648b5b451cc" id="5c17eb9e-9d8e-4499-9a96-e648b5b451cc"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="8274489a-f929-4db2-a0b5-18ba78c90f8b" id="8274489a-f929-4db2-a0b5-18ba78c90f8b"><li><p name="a42aa5b5-765e-4ee6-9644-8b52920379a8" id="a42aa5b5-765e-4ee6-9644-8b52920379a8"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="b47a75f5-3c29-4dbc-b543-af36bd90a8ba" id="b47a75f5-3c29-4dbc-b543-af36bd90a8ba"><li><p name="7a1b4d53-f5b9-4396-83ae-980a83d58631" id="7a1b4d53-f5b9-4396-83ae-980a83d58631">運動・食生活・予防医学の視点。政府の医療政策や高齢者ケアも話題。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a575bc05-693e-49cd-9b60-9f54a7d879f1" id="a575bc05-693e-49cd-9b60-9f54a7d879f1"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="fae0f6a0-db9c-4e0a-8203-ba6f28bc3f72" id="fae0f6a0-db9c-4e0a-8203-ba6f28bc3f72"><li><p name="f5087f00-356c-4109-922b-f34f163da19f" id="f5087f00-356c-4109-922b-f34f163da19f">wellness</p></li><li><p name="1321d4d5-c18c-46a5-82c4-26445de0aad5" id="1321d4d5-c18c-46a5-82c4-26445de0aad5">fitness routine</p></li><li><p name="12d82742-5005-48b9-9a47-df04ee74d1fc" id="12d82742-5005-48b9-9a47-df04ee74d1fc">preventive care</p></li><li><p name="69ae1199-46eb-4601-83d2-06576334fb16" id="69ae1199-46eb-4601-83d2-06576334fb16">healthcare system</p></li><li><p name="ae33deed-d95d-4656-885b-5b6ea56d39a8" id="ae33deed-d95d-4656-885b-5b6ea56d39a8">life expectancy など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="ed39f4d8-472f-429e-b719-4c46b665ffd7" id="ed39f4d8-472f-429e-b719-4c46b665ffd7"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="9a32cf1e-cdcc-440e-9839-b1fd3573092e" id="9a32cf1e-cdcc-440e-9839-b1fd3573092e"><li><p name="922d06bb-d08d-40b3-9c3b-e3655b7e877b" id="922d06bb-d08d-40b3-9c3b-e3655b7e877b">Q：Do you think health care should be free?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="32020ad6-226e-4852-8245-3d8130e58e2b" id="32020ad6-226e-4852-8245-3d8130e58e2b"><blockquote><p name="42df7364-8cae-499a-8e0f-7488bebac453" id="42df7364-8cae-499a-8e0f-7488bebac453">A：<br>I <strong>believe</strong> that basic health care ought to be free, because <strong>every citizen should have access</strong> to medical services. <br><strong>For instance,</strong> in many countries with free healthcare, people go for regular check-ups which prevents serious illnesses. <br><strong>On the other hand,</strong> this requires high taxes or funding. <br><strong>Personally,</strong> I think it’s a public duty to ensure health care is affordable; maybe basic care can be free while specialized treatment has a cost.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="8ef0dfa7-3d2a-4277-a140-8ee99d12112d" id="8ef0dfa7-3d2a-4277-a140-8ee99d12112d">メディア・ニュース (Media &amp; News)</h3><ul name="98f0de23-dfd9-40e0-b6a7-f56f9c685a07" id="98f0de23-dfd9-40e0-b6a7-f56f9c685a07"><li><p name="e6ed5859-6e4b-46e9-a745-22018b0f9a7b" id="e6ed5859-6e4b-46e9-a745-22018b0f9a7b"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="83502232-ed79-4771-ae28-87e3359a8ad7" id="83502232-ed79-4771-ae28-87e3359a8ad7"><li><p name="64ccd9c1-7aef-45fe-84d6-ed71a741dce3" id="64ccd9c1-7aef-45fe-84d6-ed71a741dce3">How do most people get their news in your country?</p></li><li><p name="d88fae8e-b1bf-424f-a686-419f89f21690" id="d88fae8e-b1bf-424f-a686-419f89f21690">Do you believe everything you read in the newspapers?</p></li><li><p name="41ae07e9-6f86-4490-a9e5-36c93aa7e64f" id="41ae07e9-6f86-4490-a9e5-36c93aa7e64f">How do you think people will get their news in the future?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="6f8e68cc-8722-4073-a882-4884680f7835" id="6f8e68cc-8722-4073-a882-4884680f7835"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="6f540eef-968f-4d25-b0fd-43e21afe14ac" id="6f540eef-968f-4d25-b0fd-43e21afe14ac"><li><p name="d10388c6-3443-46b1-b1e6-11358564600c" id="d10388c6-3443-46b1-b1e6-11358564600c"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="a74a6761-a440-4895-a66f-4d9de465522d" id="a74a6761-a440-4895-a66f-4d9de465522d"><li><p name="97d600cd-f323-4869-9450-33431fc5bf64" id="97d600cd-f323-4869-9450-33431fc5bf64">伝統的メディア vs インターネットメディア、情報の信憑性、フェイクニュース対策を論じる。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="e555a980-da05-416c-a3a1-1454090805d5" id="e555a980-da05-416c-a3a1-1454090805d5"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="2b1c5623-b1bb-4623-b40f-93ef3b309533" id="2b1c5623-b1bb-4623-b40f-93ef3b309533"><li><p name="18fa3f19-e6f4-4825-9e5d-e7433bc64586" id="18fa3f19-e6f4-4825-9e5d-e7433bc64586">mass media</p></li><li><p name="d97271a6-c973-4dc6-85af-91ca8ecffae9" id="d97271a6-c973-4dc6-85af-91ca8ecffae9">social media</p></li><li><p name="cba67340-1bf0-438d-af3e-d60d48e0d766" id="cba67340-1bf0-438d-af3e-d60d48e0d766">credible</p></li><li><p name="01f762dd-e126-4334-be28-4129067e3925" id="01f762dd-e126-4334-be28-4129067e3925">misinformation</p></li><li><p name="7b0562b2-ea11-4b52-bf2a-bcf8f6c1dcd6" id="7b0562b2-ea11-4b52-bf2a-bcf8f6c1dcd6">journalism など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="af1eb7e6-40c9-4cb5-8736-e55596175f08" id="af1eb7e6-40c9-4cb5-8736-e55596175f08"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="907fd127-ad33-4645-b614-52b90489ebdb" id="907fd127-ad33-4645-b614-52b90489ebdb"><li><p name="38d4bd12-92db-4658-9f94-3973e031f588" id="38d4bd12-92db-4658-9f94-3973e031f588">Q：Do you believe everything you read in newspapers?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="6c2228c1-83e8-4c79-9156-49b0484e4e4c" id="6c2228c1-83e8-4c79-9156-49b0484e4e4c"><blockquote><p name="5f8a4fc8-e432-4e29-9e1c-01b99f597b0f" id="5f8a4fc8-e432-4e29-9e1c-01b99f597b0f">A：<br>Certainly not. <br>I think some news can be biased or exaggerated. <br><strong>For example,</strong> tabloids often focus on sensational stories. <br><strong>Therefore,</strong> it’s better to cross-check information from multiple sources. <br><strong>However,</strong> reputable newspapers do have fact-checking, so I trust them more than random internet posts. <br><strong>In my view,</strong> critical thinking is crucial when consuming news.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="fa57203f-688f-455f-94a8-5a59d597732e" id="fa57203f-688f-455f-94a8-5a59d597732e">仕事 (Work)</h3><ul name="76de5887-a2f9-48b7-a0f2-a781f7bedb4e" id="76de5887-a2f9-48b7-a0f2-a781f7bedb4e"><li><p name="dad0fb07-6351-485d-908c-96b0262667dd" id="dad0fb07-6351-485d-908c-96b0262667dd"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="88c2da1c-4f49-4a60-a479-653d91f717fa" id="88c2da1c-4f49-4a60-a479-653d91f717fa"><li><p name="eb4e9f13-5480-4603-9ae9-f040d0a7c448" id="eb4e9f13-5480-4603-9ae9-f040d0a7c448">Do you think job satisfaction is more important than salary when choosing a job?</p></li><li><p name="feb2a1ae-d11f-45af-a6e3-1ca02d4f7454" id="feb2a1ae-d11f-45af-a6e3-1ca02d4f7454">What skills do you think are needed to get a good job these days?</p></li><li><p name="2008ca4c-41bb-48b7-9212-afa38ab48ff3" id="2008ca4c-41bb-48b7-9212-afa38ab48ff3">How has technology changed the way we work?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="6123e721-0dd3-42df-98b2-9f7218344430" id="6123e721-0dd3-42df-98b2-9f7218344430"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="a200f2a9-faf3-484b-bcd7-2070a586086e" id="a200f2a9-faf3-484b-bcd7-2070a586086e"><li><p name="aa29b424-e208-44b7-9762-0873d60a14bf" id="aa29b424-e208-44b7-9762-0873d60a14bf"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="1e983603-acc5-4470-8d9a-80cbf04398c4" id="1e983603-acc5-4470-8d9a-80cbf04398c4"><li><p name="37866692-96de-4c56-bb06-539490617a37" id="37866692-96de-4c56-bb06-539490617a37">仕事選びの基準（安定 vs やりがい）、リモートワークの普及やワークライフバランス。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="0de6e638-f4b0-494f-a44b-9da858757a65" id="0de6e638-f4b0-494f-a44b-9da858757a65"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="2f02c226-79d0-4265-8012-d20241ac3f77" id="2f02c226-79d0-4265-8012-d20241ac3f77"><li><p name="89ee761d-8ac2-4ea4-b0b5-e909c96821d8" id="89ee761d-8ac2-4ea4-b0b5-e909c96821d8">job satisfaction</p></li><li><p name="a032a8fc-a873-4f6d-a8a2-acdb30d97ab0" id="a032a8fc-a873-4f6d-a8a2-acdb30d97ab0">work-life balance</p></li><li><p name="e060c50a-719f-4a4c-8b08-ff487fee8dd6" id="e060c50a-719f-4a4c-8b08-ff487fee8dd6">remote work</p></li><li><p name="e285b761-e114-41ef-a4af-f38ec93b8e11" id="e285b761-e114-41ef-a4af-f38ec93b8e11">skill set</p></li><li><p name="fe9e57a6-ec8d-4367-afeb-69995be16815" id="fe9e57a6-ec8d-4367-afeb-69995be16815">career prospects など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="716608bc-2c72-4d14-9f18-186703c113c3" id="716608bc-2c72-4d14-9f18-186703c113c3"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="a0cb29b7-1e04-4783-b7d8-876a18e00044" id="a0cb29b7-1e04-4783-b7d8-876a18e00044"><li><p name="41620a4a-b019-4c5b-884c-c97ca729cfab" id="41620a4a-b019-4c5b-884c-c97ca729cfab">Q：Do you think job satisfaction is more important than salary?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="34a6492d-a545-4b46-9e24-668506a02ec9" id="34a6492d-a545-4b46-9e24-668506a02ec9"><blockquote><p name="c67f6c3c-2e30-4e7f-ba8f-8402a7ef3126" id="c67f6c3c-2e30-4e7f-ba8f-8402a7ef3126">A：<br>I <strong>would say</strong> satisfaction is more important in the long run. <br><strong>For instance,</strong> if you earn a high salary but hate the work, you might be unhappy. <br><strong>However,</strong> financial stability also matters. <br><strong>For example,</strong> a good salary can relieve stress about bills. <br><strong>Personally,</strong> I think a balance is ideal: a decent income <strong>and</strong> a job you enjoy.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="4b3f8109-90a5-419c-92f3-7d313047eaff" id="4b3f8109-90a5-419c-92f3-7d313047eaff">グローバリゼーション (Globalization)</h3><ul name="7d848fa1-15a4-472f-962e-053fc8d2d33c" id="7d848fa1-15a4-472f-962e-053fc8d2d33c"><li><p name="6d5d794e-1d9b-4552-8f35-73ba76859049" id="6d5d794e-1d9b-4552-8f35-73ba76859049"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="101183dc-fc22-454e-8eb7-5be9ec98678e" id="101183dc-fc22-454e-8eb7-5be9ec98678e"><li><p name="733f2e22-79e2-411b-904c-860b9635c8d9" id="733f2e22-79e2-411b-904c-860b9635c8d9">Has globalization affected small businesses in your country?</p></li><li><p name="0b26e194-94b0-4193-88a8-f6a1bd506d18" id="0b26e194-94b0-4193-88a8-f6a1bd506d18">What are the advantages or disadvantages of globalization?</p></li><li><p name="4a54d3bf-e65a-4bd5-bb80-6232233fa477" id="4a54d3bf-e65a-4bd5-bb80-6232233fa477">Do you think international trade is always good?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="7b4ee99b-6964-4038-9804-52d100cb4d5a" id="7b4ee99b-6964-4038-9804-52d100cb4d5a"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="61d842c8-ad0b-42f7-9d6d-75fde5c7b081" id="61d842c8-ad0b-42f7-9d6d-75fde5c7b081"><li><p name="29a3b806-68f5-4ce3-8ebc-c4c5a30c0859" id="29a3b806-68f5-4ce3-8ebc-c4c5a30c0859"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="ac7976d0-9fcf-4f1f-9506-aca4b765b497" id="ac7976d0-9fcf-4f1f-9506-aca4b765b497"><li><p name="2aef4295-937e-432c-923e-3ebcc0a31aae" id="2aef4295-937e-432c-923e-3ebcc0a31aae">グローバル化による市場拡大と文化摩擦、地元産業への影響。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="5a2ba907-eb3e-428e-8ffa-42455cc034cd" id="5a2ba907-eb3e-428e-8ffa-42455cc034cd"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="9654bfa9-aec4-4ec6-98fa-f7f06e00d287" id="9654bfa9-aec4-4ec6-98fa-f7f06e00d287"><li><p name="abe31004-a530-4adb-b25c-7e493ff133c3" id="abe31004-a530-4adb-b25c-7e493ff133c3">international trade</p></li><li><p name="a69cd0bf-59b4-40d4-b04f-601ff9422af3" id="a69cd0bf-59b4-40d4-b04f-601ff9422af3">local economy</p></li><li><p name="69c71986-3b13-4bea-a60e-9b2cf5bde3b9" id="69c71986-3b13-4bea-a60e-9b2cf5bde3b9">cultural exchange</p></li><li><p name="c8bb98c7-ae9e-4162-a8d4-d1af607142f2" id="c8bb98c7-ae9e-4162-a8d4-d1af607142f2">competition, economy など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="5f1a06d9-f54d-4832-99d7-7e9b9788c4e9" id="5f1a06d9-f54d-4832-99d7-7e9b9788c4e9"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="2864bf30-908e-495d-89b0-0ead632a949c" id="2864bf30-908e-495d-89b0-0ead632a949c"><li><p name="309d87c1-3539-4b94-b58f-4f3254fb58a2" id="309d87c1-3539-4b94-b58f-4f3254fb58a2">Q：Has globalization affected small businesses?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="87defbaa-8b62-4894-9272-eab19bc840ef" id="87defbaa-8b62-4894-9272-eab19bc840ef"><blockquote><p name="c64e6ee4-41de-419f-b149-48312499982d" id="c64e6ee4-41de-419f-b149-48312499982d">A：<br>Yes, <strong>in both ways</strong>. <br><strong>On the one hand,</strong> it has opened new markets – local crafts can be sold abroad online. <br><strong>On the other hand,</strong> small shops face more competition from international brands. <br><strong>For example,</strong> local stores sometimes can’t compete with cheaper imported goods. <br><strong>Therefore,</strong> governments may need to support small businesses. <br><strong>Personally,</strong> I think globalization offers opportunity but also requires caution.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="26350263-ac99-4dd9-9a1c-bbf691dc412c" id="26350263-ac99-4dd9-9a1c-bbf691dc412c">高齢化 (Ageing Population)</h3><ul name="17fa9671-ab1c-4cd2-b1ac-b0baab80c54e" id="17fa9671-ab1c-4cd2-b1ac-b0baab80c54e"><li><p name="b4c78df3-2afa-4679-8574-fe8d9ec4fc16" id="b4c78df3-2afa-4679-8574-fe8d9ec4fc16"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="440167da-ae3c-4e0d-93ab-f3160ab67d51" id="440167da-ae3c-4e0d-93ab-f3160ab67d51"><li><p name="fac11dd9-8f91-4e07-9a9e-39f2f7345314" id="fac11dd9-8f91-4e07-9a9e-39f2f7345314">Who should be responsible for the care of the elderly, the family or the government?</p></li><li><p name="01d9dfa9-45ed-433e-9ff8-86e346feef0d" id="01d9dfa9-45ed-433e-9ff8-86e346feef0d">What problems does an ageing population cause?</p></li><li><p name="e710f722-463f-453c-a6f6-b21dc77a1225" id="e710f722-463f-453c-a6f6-b21dc77a1225">Are there benefits to having a larger elderly population?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="a68cc658-4f47-4b2d-80ae-d6ccf7448ec9" id="a68cc658-4f47-4b2d-80ae-d6ccf7448ec9"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="760e9e84-bbb2-4bc0-a89f-f5f8909ac76d" id="760e9e84-bbb2-4bc0-a89f-f5f8909ac76d"><li><p name="bb1c73fc-de99-43b0-b5e7-00ba4ec82ba5" id="bb1c73fc-de99-43b0-b5e7-00ba4ec82ba5"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="e68f72b3-5b5d-40c5-b980-15c80bab2e18" id="e68f72b3-5b5d-40c5-b980-15c80bab2e18"><li><p name="cdcb51d6-0ae1-43ed-8310-6579089d8107" id="cdcb51d6-0ae1-43ed-8310-6579089d8107">高齢社会の課題（年金、介護）と高齢者の貢献（経験やボランティア）。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="998a48aa-238d-4ba5-a8e3-358ca97692e3" id="998a48aa-238d-4ba5-a8e3-358ca97692e3"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="7374767b-b6cc-4fd9-abb0-9f76f8230c95" id="7374767b-b6cc-4fd9-abb0-9f76f8230c95"><li><p name="b9096334-ad49-47e1-ba82-a588f5022f67" id="b9096334-ad49-47e1-ba82-a588f5022f67">retirement age</p></li><li><p name="cafa237f-5a2d-46fc-8324-596bd281147b" id="cafa237f-5a2d-46fc-8324-596bd281147b">pension system</p></li><li><p name="dd4a50b6-464b-4eb5-b7ad-d5cedfb551c1" id="dd4a50b6-464b-4eb5-b7ad-d5cedfb551c1">healthcare services</p></li><li><p name="e1c81fa2-0d36-491d-832e-e043325d0016" id="e1c81fa2-0d36-491d-832e-e043325d0016">elderly care</p></li><li><p name="7e734530-7eed-4133-8560-f4bb23769087" id="7e734530-7eed-4133-8560-f4bb23769087">social security など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="e7933220-1c73-4403-aaf9-8132ebe4536d" id="e7933220-1c73-4403-aaf9-8132ebe4536d"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="e7a332c0-0784-47e0-bdaf-01c792e91ba8" id="e7a332c0-0784-47e0-bdaf-01c792e91ba8"><li><p name="f62960ea-60b6-45a5-9a2e-0efb068a5ee0" id="f62960ea-60b6-45a5-9a2e-0efb068a5ee0">Q：Who should care for the elderly, family or government?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="50157bce-b98c-42d9-ab96-56071ebc8bf7" id="50157bce-b98c-42d9-ab96-56071ebc8bf7"><blockquote><p name="d29952b9-6ecf-41e2-a674-4b1a06ba51dd" id="d29952b9-6ecf-41e2-a674-4b1a06ba51dd">A：<br>It’s a <strong>shared responsibility</strong>. <br><strong>Traditionally,</strong> families took care of elders, which is important for emotional support. <br><strong>For example,</strong> grandparents often help with childcare. <br><strong>However,</strong> not all families have resources, so <strong>the government</strong> should provide social security and eldercare services. <br><strong>Personally,</strong> I think both play a role: family love plus government support.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="c8450b7c-890b-4901-85b1-6d1e195713f9" id="c8450b7c-890b-4901-85b1-6d1e195713f9">文化・社会 (Culture/Society)</h3><ul name="cd0985c9-0d4a-479c-a966-25b77fdb55e4" id="cd0985c9-0d4a-479c-a966-25b77fdb55e4"><li><p name="82fb68dd-c0df-4eea-b038-443bf8649bb4" id="82fb68dd-c0df-4eea-b038-443bf8649bb4"><strong>質問例：</strong></p><ul name="d57388e7-e5ea-48dc-9561-b848a5f5da82" id="d57388e7-e5ea-48dc-9561-b848a5f5da82"><li><p name="4ac8e09d-d5a9-4a60-81fe-22e9c73ba969" id="4ac8e09d-d5a9-4a60-81fe-22e9c73ba969">How has your country’s culture changed over the last few decades?</p></li><li><p name="a1c083a3-b4dc-4b79-a8ed-615ddbd5c99f" id="a1c083a3-b4dc-4b79-a8ed-615ddbd5c99f">Do you think it’s important to keep traditions alive?</p></li><li><p name="29f553ba-3e4f-4d09-947d-50d16086b148" id="29f553ba-3e4f-4d09-947d-50d16086b148">What social problems are there in your country?</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="c0bd5f6c-0dfa-4356-baf7-51699fed1bc2" id="c0bd5f6c-0dfa-4356-baf7-51699fed1bc2"><strong>対策・語彙：</strong></p><ul name="206269fd-453d-46ed-b911-d518017d22c5" id="206269fd-453d-46ed-b911-d518017d22c5"><li><p name="944615ad-c42c-473e-8c7b-1c936fe212e5" id="944615ad-c42c-473e-8c7b-1c936fe212e5"><strong>答えの切り口：</strong></p><ul name="04ab103e-ba50-4d45-8685-57552076aa70" id="04ab103e-ba50-4d45-8685-57552076aa70"><li><p name="3469b19a-6b59-4039-9a78-d7b6188beac2" id="3469b19a-6b59-4039-9a78-d7b6188beac2">伝統 vs 現代化の葛藤、グローバル化による文化交流、貧困・教育格差など社会課題への意識。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="efd97324-5343-4cc3-9939-0760d91cd268" id="efd97324-5343-4cc3-9939-0760d91cd268"><strong>語彙例：</strong></p><ul name="3c6e7abb-2f05-409a-9055-6e91ac907701" id="3c6e7abb-2f05-409a-9055-6e91ac907701"><li><p name="1623e40a-a251-401e-bbf4-df42b2c1154a" id="1623e40a-a251-401e-bbf4-df42b2c1154a">tradition</p></li><li><p name="19d57d0c-b292-418f-a805-af54ef0421e6" id="19d57d0c-b292-418f-a805-af54ef0421e6">modernization</p></li><li><p name="23a306d8-793b-4f77-ad39-98620c6a27ba" id="23a306d8-793b-4f77-ad39-98620c6a27ba">globalization</p></li><li><p name="5fa8cf79-0617-4885-8de8-ec4273ed637b" id="5fa8cf79-0617-4885-8de8-ec4273ed637b">inequality</p></li><li><p name="c8524a9f-11cd-43f9-bc9c-6c5650ae0a9f" id="c8524a9f-11cd-43f9-bc9c-6c5650ae0a9f">poverty</p></li><li><p name="b42dede8-affc-4970-a27c-a9a9e85637eb" id="b42dede8-affc-4970-a27c-a9a9e85637eb">charity など。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="2ec6a944-e60f-4ad5-a49e-011e15312230" id="2ec6a944-e60f-4ad5-a49e-011e15312230"><strong>模範回答例：</strong></p><ul name="e88f3f4e-9f79-4b59-b280-62e8a6071499" id="e88f3f4e-9f79-4b59-b280-62e8a6071499"><li><p name="6c515fbc-641e-46b5-bc93-06bc2fc5c535" id="6c515fbc-641e-46b5-bc93-06bc2fc5c535">Q：What can be done to alleviate poverty?</p></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="02b3f130-7c18-423f-a8de-6b78ddcab474" id="02b3f130-7c18-423f-a8de-6b78ddcab474"><blockquote><p name="bb5ff98a-a4fa-49bf-9b84-922fbc98c555" id="bb5ff98a-a4fa-49bf-9b84-922fbc98c555">A：<br>Improving education and job opportunities is crucial. <br><strong>For instance,</strong> providing vocational training helps people find jobs. <br><strong>At the same time,</strong> charities and government programs can offer temporary support. <br><strong>Overall,</strong> a combination of social programs and personal initiative is needed.</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><hr><h3 name="00d8dd66-5d85-4ce8-95ee-b7383000cd8a" id="00d8dd66-5d85-4ce8-95ee-b7383000cd8a">その他のトピック例</h3><ul name="30b3d5a5-0038-40fc-aefb-5226da0c032c" id="30b3d5a5-0038-40fc-aefb-5226da0c032c"><li><p name="f2a5da06-8add-4966-97ac-9e1ddc690c75" id="f2a5da06-8add-4966-97ac-9e1ddc690c75"><strong>旅行・交通 (Travel/Transport)：</strong></p><ul name="aed72a92-32c6-480a-a8ed-6c8e39a3d3f6" id="aed72a92-32c6-480a-a8ed-6c8e39a3d3f6"><li><p name="ff507e22-3938-41b2-80f5-0d006d8ad9d7" id="ff507e22-3938-41b2-80f5-0d006d8ad9d7">Why do people prefer to travel abroad rather than their own country?など。</p></li><li><p name="e4e5393f-1a3f-4bc6-ad69-3d2521dc0d9d" id="e4e5393f-1a3f-4bc6-ad69-3d2521dc0d9d">交通手段の発展や安全性の変化について。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="9cec2290-68b3-42e1-aa00-82702fde8b01" id="9cec2290-68b3-42e1-aa00-82702fde8b01"><strong>メディア・広告 (Advertising/Media)：</strong></p><ul name="4ff3f8b0-0a85-4e00-b00e-99299b3112a1" id="4ff3f8b0-0a85-4e00-b00e-99299b3112a1"><li><p name="6720666d-ec66-43ba-9c6c-7fad34987d4a" id="6720666d-ec66-43ba-9c6c-7fad34987d4a">Do you think advertising aimed at children is acceptable?など。</p></li><li><p name="f0fa4ca5-0f31-4949-a6df-502750baa0cd" id="f0fa4ca5-0f31-4949-a6df-502750baa0cd">情報・宣伝の影響力について。</p></li></ul></li><li><p name="0f37af4c-642c-42ba-b43f-cee03a947f7c" id="0f37af4c-642c-42ba-b43f-cee03a947f7c"><strong>社会的意思決定 (Decision Making)：</strong></p><ul name="ab15c5ff-48ef-49e3-8b5e-922fc6168725" id="ab15c5ff-48ef-49e3-8b5e-922fc6168725"><li><p name="46b5151e-1c81-4cbe-a1a1-f638e85593d0" id="46b5151e-1c81-4cbe-a1a1-f638e85593d0">Why do some people find it difficult to make big decisions?など。</p></li><li><p name="f05cbb31-940a-4592-b293-752eb2f86d07" id="f05cbb31-940a-4592-b293-752eb2f86d07">意思決定のプロセスやアドバイスの重要性について。</p></li></ul></li></ul><p name="410e9371-1b88-477c-bf38-f47f566195d7" id="410e9371-1b88-477c-bf38-f47f566195d7">上記各トピックでは、まず<strong>質問のキーワード</strong>（過去形・現在形・未来形、比較表現など）に注意して質問の本質を把握し、次に前出の必勝フレーズで論理立てて答えを展開します。<br><br>例えば環境問題なら「環境を守るためには何をするべきか？」と尋ねられれば、“Individuals can recycle and conserve energy. For example, many people now install solar panels. However, government policies are also needed.” のように回答します。</p><figure name="833cfea2-ac89-4d52-834c-ed991c7928a5" id="833cfea2-ac89-4d52-834c-ed991c7928a5"><blockquote><p name="a000a918-a18a-4637-a0be-44ce0f6aec9d" id="a000a918-a18a-4637-a0be-44ce0f6aec9d">参考：<br>・各トピックの質問例はIELTS対策サイトで多数紹介されています。<br>・例えば教育問題では「Do you think computers will one day replace teachers?」、仕事では「Do you think job satisfaction is more important than salary?」などが典型的です。</p></blockquote><figcaption></figcaption></figure><p name="208dd010-1b9d-4585-9757-d4510e36e86a" id="208dd010-1b9d-4585-9757-d4510e36e86a">以上のように、設問パターンを意識したフレーズとトピック別対策を組み合わせることで、Part3での論理的な回答力が高まります。<br>論点を明確に示し、根拠や例を交えた回答を心がけましょう。</p><hr><h2 name="24797bee-f9ca-49b0-9803-4564fa13a541" id="24797bee-f9ca-49b0-9803-4564fa13a541">フィルター表現・パラフレーズ・ヘッジの活用</h2><figure name="ffa00199-6d72-4776-9205-69528f31f9f5" id="ffa00199-6d72-4776-9205-69528f31f9f5"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993632-sqgQ2Bc8tYpzWVEJef1MjrCi.png" alt="" width="620" height="345"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><ul name="6fcb3232-eb4f-4501-b7ab-b03ed1806083" id="6fcb3232-eb4f-4501-b7ab-b03ed1806083"><li><p name="e8918e38-dd40-4be4-9431-6b1c0de5c7ef" id="e8918e38-dd40-4be4-9431-6b1c0de5c7ef"><strong>フィルター表現</strong>：</p><ul name="d294d3a5-e32d-4a8d-9ff1-4ee2ced37b44" id="d294d3a5-e32d-4a8d-9ff1-4ee2ced37b44"><li><p name="99f0efdd-fdc1-4109-8197-f498f5816087" id="99f0efdd-fdc1-4109-8197-f498f5816087">話の始めに</p><ul name="12175ff5-816c-48a0-87e1-8b88521759ce" id="12175ff5-816c-48a0-87e1-8b88521759ce"><li><p name="b7f6ea31-8d85-4413-b7b3-1e3212f34188" id="b7f6ea31-8d85-4413-b7b3-1e3212f34188">“To be honest,”「正直言って」</p></li><li><p name="c64ff09b-e3c7-42e7-a84d-9b43b4a173fa" id="c64ff09b-e3c7-42e7-a84d-9b43b4a173fa">“Well,”「ええと」</p></li><li><p name="147e448b-4a0e-4223-bdc0-3bbe96950e56" id="147e448b-4a0e-4223-bdc0-3bbe96950e56">“I mean,”「つまり」などを使うと自然な口調になります。</p><ul name="e6a5495d-1ef2-49d2-9684-7c149c678e11" id="e6a5495d-1ef2-49d2-9684-7c149c678e11"><li><p name="8cfccc3e-bf3e-4cd4-80d2-f194e6b25411" id="8cfccc3e-bf3e-4cd4-80d2-f194e6b25411">ただし多用は控えましょう。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="8eea390f-4dff-4ec4-ab83-baa58ffee2ce" id="8eea390f-4dff-4ec4-ab83-baa58ffee2ce"><strong>ヘッジ</strong>：</p><ul name="e426d8c8-ce0d-433c-9d98-919e29f9a32f" id="e426d8c8-ce0d-433c-9d98-919e29f9a32f"><li><p name="949462b9-746c-4341-95b6-6a1d916986d4" id="949462b9-746c-4341-95b6-6a1d916986d4">自信を持っていない事柄には</p><ul name="95a63305-754f-41a9-ac7b-7cdb0641c3f0" id="95a63305-754f-41a9-ac7b-7cdb0641c3f0"><li><p name="10a1a464-6319-4ee2-bbb1-ebea4065d5be" id="10a1a464-6319-4ee2-bbb1-ebea4065d5be">“perhaps”「おそらく」</p></li><li><p name="b947b373-e6cc-41eb-af63-d900f2cec6fc" id="b947b373-e6cc-41eb-af63-d900f2cec6fc">“I guess”「～だと思います」</p></li><li><p name="d8ef7c9c-9a8c-461c-8d53-676b4400a6fe" id="d8ef7c9c-9a8c-461c-8d53-676b4400a6fe">“some people say”「～という人もいます」</p></li><li><p name="78e9b1db-5b86-4272-8618-6fd20ec7e195" id="78e9b1db-5b86-4272-8618-6fd20ec7e195">“kind of”「～のような感じで」などを使って調整します。</p><ul name="ba8bfc26-838d-41c2-b2bf-c3ea8085f6f0" id="ba8bfc26-838d-41c2-b2bf-c3ea8085f6f0"><li><p name="c1dfd482-5abd-4a16-a5a3-04090f33e434" id="c1dfd482-5abd-4a16-a5a3-04090f33e434">断定を避けつつ柔らかい印象になります。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul><figure name="7f3bd110-dd11-4212-9ad8-96343dce1767" id="7f3bd110-dd11-4212-9ad8-96343dce1767"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993656-GEa8eKBSMQRYFlN4AvqWX6OZ.png" alt="" width="620" height="375"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><ul name="153f4ab6-7b5a-4b76-84a7-528ba4a9dcd5" id="153f4ab6-7b5a-4b76-84a7-528ba4a9dcd5"><li><p name="35c93627-8676-4f61-80f3-318379c87b23" id="35c93627-8676-4f61-80f3-318379c87b23"><strong>パラフレーズ</strong>：</p><ul name="91ad0b01-c3fa-4f7d-b279-484982c9d00e" id="91ad0b01-c3fa-4f7d-b279-484982c9d00e"><li><p name="a9bd0a3f-3b1d-463c-9544-c0ae1fb7f45f" id="a9bd0a3f-3b1d-463c-9544-c0ae1fb7f45f">同じ単語を繰り返さないように、別の言い方で言い換えます（例：big → <strong>huge</strong>, important → <strong>significant</strong>）。</p><ul name="a8a4184a-8e3c-4ee3-8288-a618d691f2e0" id="a8a4184a-8e3c-4ee3-8288-a618d691f2e0"><li><p name="81d55442-6b92-4e8c-9a8f-4dc268bfd091" id="81d55442-6b92-4e8c-9a8f-4dc268bfd091">質問の表現をそのまま使わずに言い換えることで、語彙の幅を示せます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h2 name="dd6fb1c4-25e4-466f-8cf7-9e50c1f981f8" id="dd6fb1c4-25e4-466f-8cf7-9e50c1f981f8">まとめ：バンド7.0獲得のための総まとめ</h2><figure name="18754d87-59e0-49b6-be7c-deadab57145f" id="18754d87-59e0-49b6-be7c-deadab57145f"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993680-qPNZRMSAlETBQKxcXz02eLIG.png" alt="" width="620" height="344"><figcaption></figcaption></figure><ul name="9d77b5a5-537f-42bf-9e11-d5eb0e651e5d" id="9d77b5a5-537f-42bf-9e11-d5eb0e651e5d"><li><p name="64eae090-71ba-4289-8f7f-a29d48cfc208" id="64eae090-71ba-4289-8f7f-a29d48cfc208"><strong>論理的構成</strong>：</p><ul name="9104bcc3-b287-403e-a5ea-762aa0d6f0c8" id="9104bcc3-b287-403e-a5ea-762aa0d6f0c8"><li><p name="9a483b41-0c76-4793-8f55-53b4b9255827" id="9a483b41-0c76-4793-8f55-53b4b9255827">回答は序論→本論→結論の流れで一貫した論理展開を保ちます。</p><ul name="342a9616-2677-4065-b18a-f960748e0729" id="342a9616-2677-4065-b18a-f960748e0729"><li><p name="69800600-36e3-4de5-87f7-9b510b40fb34" id="69800600-36e3-4de5-87f7-9b510b40fb34">例示や説明を段階的に重ね、締め括りで自分の意見を再確認しましょう。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="9b594eb7-9fe1-46d1-94bd-315afea1626c" id="9b594eb7-9fe1-46d1-94bd-315afea1626c"><strong>十分な詳細</strong>：</p><ul name="359b2210-82a0-4743-8613-a5fa70059acb" id="359b2210-82a0-4743-8613-a5fa70059acb"><li><p name="19f56c42-fbe8-4d2c-96de-5c541f8a0afe" id="19f56c42-fbe8-4d2c-96de-5c541f8a0afe">可能な限り具体的な情報（数字、状況、エピソード）を付け加え、回答の深みを増します。</p><ul name="9bb1dfad-95f2-4d24-8e0a-b78fa55de763" id="9bb1dfad-95f2-4d24-8e0a-b78fa55de763"><li><p name="3c00deb3-77b6-4476-8a77-4b1925d2708a" id="3c00deb3-77b6-4476-8a77-4b1925d2708a">ただし、脱線や意味のない繰り返しは避けます。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="2d8bf5cd-cc81-47ad-bf4a-0176655a59bb" id="2d8bf5cd-cc81-47ad-bf4a-0176655a59bb"><strong>接続詞・ディスコースマーカー</strong>：</p><ul name="9e3b287b-2127-41a0-9f1f-3b04275515fb" id="9e3b287b-2127-41a0-9f1f-3b04275515fb"><li><p name="41e895f3-0f15-4f15-962b-00e6d80d9e9a" id="41e895f3-0f15-4f15-962b-00e6d80d9e9a">“For example,” “Moreover,” “However,” “Therefore,” “On the other hand,” などの接続表現を適切に用い、文と文をつなげます。</p><ul name="ecd5217f-be5d-4ba9-ad71-c3375f8e4acf" id="ecd5217f-be5d-4ba9-ad71-c3375f8e4acf"><li><p name="ee369168-cb24-4316-ba80-77b408c569f3" id="ee369168-cb24-4316-ba80-77b408c569f3">過剰にならないよう自然に配置し、英語らしい流れを作りましょう。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="0b596a7f-2950-4fe0-8e93-a74786a981ff" id="0b596a7f-2950-4fe0-8e93-a74786a981ff"><strong>豊富な語彙</strong>：</p><ul name="af696bef-c868-463a-859a-5dc12eebe5c5" id="af696bef-c868-463a-859a-5dc12eebe5c5"><li><p name="c3d4efcd-29ef-4e3f-874a-d1413a64053f" id="c3d4efcd-29ef-4e3f-874a-d1413a64053f">幅広いボキャブラリーを使い、必要に応じて同義語で言い換えます。</p><ul name="eaf25063-7b5e-4149-8167-a87b25294416" id="eaf25063-7b5e-4149-8167-a87b25294416"><li><p name="c619976c-7d14-428b-b6e8-445737eccd12" id="c619976c-7d14-428b-b6e8-445737eccd12">慣用句やコロケーション（例：make a decision, become aware of など）も適度に取り入れると印象が良いです。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="70ebaea6-e886-4522-83ad-d2984c179624" id="70ebaea6-e886-4522-83ad-d2984c179624"><strong>複雑文の活用</strong>：</p><ul name="84384e4d-29f4-43c0-b0ee-b9c8d12fcc6e" id="84384e4d-29f4-43c0-b0ee-b9c8d12fcc6e"><li><p name="b074e34c-c64c-4a35-a9e3-7ea54bb1642b" id="b074e34c-c64c-4a35-a9e3-7ea54bb1642b">関係代名詞節、条件節、譲歩節などを織り交ぜた複文を使いましょう。</p><ul name="f0058042-3489-4829-837d-76b8e3db6549" id="f0058042-3489-4829-837d-76b8e3db6549"><li><p name="b3e24fdd-49a3-4f54-a379-6a277267082c" id="b3e24fdd-49a3-4f54-a379-6a277267082c">バンド7では「複数の複雑構文を柔軟に使う」ことが求められます。</p></li><li><p name="bb33ab79-34ab-403e-8ac9-7137f4062528" id="bb33ab79-34ab-403e-8ac9-7137f4062528">ミスに注意しつつ、長めの文にも挑戦します。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="bb6edb95-f4ed-4f8d-879b-d35fcdbf005a" id="bb6edb95-f4ed-4f8d-879b-d35fcdbf005a"><strong>声と発音</strong>：</p><ul name="0ed5c4b8-fde5-4af5-9ec7-e7cf095c0afd" id="0ed5c4b8-fde5-4af5-9ec7-e7cf095c0afd"><li><p name="0b810a7e-a402-4081-879e-520d592905fa" id="0b810a7e-a402-4081-879e-520d592905fa">はっきりとした声で話し、適切なイントネーションやストレスを意識します。</p><ul name="a69df146-8b1a-4138-ad1e-dc9ca11f6185" id="a69df146-8b1a-4138-ad1e-dc9ca11f6185"><li><p name="a6695973-8abe-4a2a-b552-95d6d0185755" id="a6695973-8abe-4a2a-b552-95d6d0185755">不要な沈黙や早口は避け、リズムよく話す練習をしましょう。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="deff12ba-b994-4369-940e-3ef042a6e140" id="deff12ba-b994-4369-940e-3ef042a6e140"><strong>練習</strong>：</p><ul name="6822a217-1a85-4a3b-a57a-0b7b0fa9b3c3" id="6822a217-1a85-4a3b-a57a-0b7b0fa9b3c3"><li><p name="c9fa7614-87e0-4c30-aa68-a574798110e7" id="c9fa7614-87e0-4c30-aa68-a574798110e7">録音して聞き返したり、模擬試験で時間内に話す練習を重ねます。</p><ul name="3dbc0eb4-7fa1-40fd-877c-23201f3b42f4" id="3dbc0eb4-7fa1-40fd-877c-23201f3b42f4"><li><p name="b47d205f-efd3-4d57-bbde-6f878d581777" id="b47d205f-efd3-4d57-bbde-6f878d581777">自分の答えを客観的に評価し、改善点を見つけましょう。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="6e479fd7-3465-4c5c-bb7c-bc49bbde9b71" id="6e479fd7-3465-4c5c-bb7c-bc49bbde9b71"><strong>5W1Hを活用</strong>：</p><ul name="ad539055-b598-44dd-aee6-bd0c9f91fcee" id="ad539055-b598-44dd-aee6-bd0c9f91fcee"><li><p name="f4d01573-f42a-4fa2-bf71-84239a920bb2" id="f4d01573-f42a-4fa2-bf71-84239a920bb2">回答の際は「いつ・どこで・誰と・何を・なぜ・どのように」を意識し、多角的な情報を盛り込みます。</p><ul name="b878ddce-422c-4aab-be5b-8057df053203" id="b878ddce-422c-4aab-be5b-8057df053203"><li><p name="0cf982ef-5760-485c-9780-c8cd361049c9" id="0cf982ef-5760-485c-9780-c8cd361049c9">特にPart2では状況設定、Part3では背景説明の要素が効果的です。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li><li><p name="a3d56e12-031d-49ba-864b-5c372131d715" id="a3d56e12-031d-49ba-864b-5c372131d715"><strong>個人的視点と一般論のバランス</strong>：</p><ul name="b2e5e30c-0dcc-4206-9f5b-3eb3acdac5df" id="b2e5e30c-0dcc-4206-9f5b-3eb3acdac5df"><li><p name="82ff9c61-a68c-44c2-822d-5bd5f7f08485" id="82ff9c61-a68c-44c2-822d-5bd5f7f08485">自分自身の経験や感想だけでなく、一般的な考えや他者の例も織り交ぜると説得力が増します。</p><ul name="6b5981cd-542c-497c-8ca4-86ef9ff713d2" id="6b5981cd-542c-497c-8ca4-86ef9ff713d2"><li><p name="77cead95-5c4c-4b1b-8e2f-5bcdaa14b33b" id="77cead95-5c4c-4b1b-8e2f-5bcdaa14b33b">たとえば「私の場合は～だが、一般的には～」と述べる練習をしましょう。</p></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul><hr><figure name="05786853-2219-4413-a76f-dc25a0bd1d03" id="05786853-2219-4413-a76f-dc25a0bd1d03"><img src="/assets/ne68beb472a95_1750993699-5woUvVmPgEtL82NKa6ChXync.png" alt="" width="620" height="350"><figcaption>是非、こちらもご参照ください。</figcaption></figure><p name="ee1aec83-5de8-4169-a266-e9f42fd89c41" id="ee1aec83-5de8-4169-a266-e9f42fd89c41">以上のポイントを踏まえ、各パートで練習と対策を徹底すれば、バンド7.0に必要な英語力と受験スキルを確実に身につけられます。<br><br>論理的で豊かな表現を磨き、試験当日は自信を持って話しましょう。<br><br>頑張ってください！</p>
